Kaiser Wilhelm II's 'Lost Conversation': Once Advocated German-American Alliance Against Japan, Revisiting an Incident from 1908, Harboring Intent to Annihilate Japan, Viewing England as a Traitor to the White Race 18

Boston: Mr. Harry is now publishing Kaiser Wilhelm II's 'Lost Conversation' with his father in 1908, at the height of his power. At that time, Wilhelm II advocated a German-American alliance to deal with the emerging Japan in Asia. This famous conversation will be published in the May issue of the Atlantic Monthly. The Associated Press has obtained the contents of this valuable and famous conversation from the magazine, and a summary is as follows: In 1905, when Wilhelm II heard that Russia had been defeated by Japan, he was deeply saddened. He sighed and said, "I wish my ships could have the opportunity to fight Japan, but this would be effortless. We must never allow China and Japan to unite, and we must never allow Japan to annex China. This is the special mission of our white race today. We don't need to talk about Britain, because England is a traitor to the white race." The conversation was too revealing, so the German Foreign Ministry did not allow it to be published publicly, but submitted a reviewed draft to Century Magazine for publication. However, it was withdrawn before publication. The world became aware of this conversation. For twenty-six years, publishers have repeatedly tried to obtain this manuscript, but have failed. Therefore, this 'Lost Conversation' has become a famous manuscript with significant historical value. In this conversation, Wilhelm II also said, "Everyone knows that there will be a conflict between the yellow race and the white race one day. If we forget our sacred duty and fail to preserve our inherent civilization and the religion given to us by God, then we will have no face to face our ancestors. We all know that the Japanese hate the white race even more than the white race hates demons. The Japanese are demons. This is a straightforward statement." He then talked about the results of his several meetings with former U.S. President Roosevelt. Wilhelm II said, "There will be a day when the world will realize what our transatlantic neighbors think when they read the joint German-American declaration to protect China's sovereignty. In my observation, the future of the world will belong to the Anglo-Teutonic nations of Northern Europe, and you Americans are also of this nation." (National Telegram, 20th)

Russia Increases Purchases of British Goods: Six Times Higher Than Last Year 21

(London) According to statistics released today by the Moscow Narodny Bank, Soviet Russia's purchases of goods from the United Kingdom this year have increased compared to last year. The total value of Soviet Russia's purchases from the UK in March this year increased sixfold compared to the same month last year, totaling approximately £907,688. The total value of Russian purchases from the UK in the first three months of this year was £2,260,317, compared to £1,271,922 for the same period last year. The most significant increases were in the purchase of machinery, electrical materials, rubber, and cotton textiles, especially in cotton textiles. Although the number of British purchases of woolens is not yet known, it is not much different from the number of Soviet Russian purchases of British goods. According to Russian officials, due to Congressman Johnson's proposal to ban loans to countries that do not fulfill their debt obligations, Soviet Russia has switched to ordering many goods from the United Kingdom instead of the United States. (Reuters, 20th)

Roosevelt: Will Not Allow Purchase of Silver, Most Silver Proposals Rejected 33

(Washington) The White House announced today that President Roosevelt has decided to reject plans to purchase large quantities of silver in order to raise world prices, and therefore the President will not approve most of the silver bills in this Congress. The White House also said that the President does not want this Congress to enact any further silver bills or new silver proposals. The Congressional Silver Conference is scheduled to meet tomorrow, but whether it has been invited by the President is now a difficult question. It is rumored that the General Assembly has already convened the conference, but it has been denied by the President. According to President Roosevelt, he only allows the silver senators to send a representative to attend. Therefore, it is worth pondering how the silver conference will proceed tomorrow. (National Telegram, 20th)

(Washington) Senator King convened a meeting of the Silver Committee this morning to draft the procedures to be submitted to President Roosevelt. Silver leaders denied that they had accepted the permissive rather than mandatory legislation. Senator Borah said today that he did not want to hear about permissive legislation and did not want to attend the White House meeting. According to White House sources, President Roosevelt felt that the issue of silver currency recovery had already been discussed in the program submitted to the London World Economic Conference in June last year. According to this program, all countries would determine the amount of silver as reserves based on their gold supply. President Roosevelt also believed that this matter could not be handled by one country without the cooperation of other countries. President Roosevelt will consult with silver senators tomorrow, but judging from President Roosevelt's views, he will probably oppose the establishment of mandatory legislation during this congressional session. (Reuters, 20th)

(Washington) President Roosevelt and the Silver Senators are scheduled to meet tomorrow, but according to White House sources tonight, President Roosevelt does not want to introduce any legislation on silver during this congressional session. President Roosevelt believes that silver is a matter of international negotiation, not a national action. (Reuters, 20th)

(Washington) President Roosevelt today approved the plan proposed by Congressman Bankhead and Senator Glass for the Federal Reserve Banks to directly lend to industries to help them recover, aimed at promoting President Roosevelt's policy of making jobs available to all citizens. Industries that must borrow in order to reduce working hours and increase employment can request loans from the Reserve Banks. The plan provides for the establishment of an industrial advisory committee in each Federal Reserve district to review loan requests. The term of each loan is five years. The initiators of this plan, Bankhead and Glass, have both been instructed by President Roosevelt to advance this plan in both houses. (Reuters, 20th)

San Diego, California: Five U.S. Navy aircraft departed from the North Island Naval Air Station today for Alaska to conduct detailed surveys along the Aleutian Islands. U.S. Naval Circles Believe it Involves Internal Affairs 35

(New York) Former Chairman of the Naval Committee Breedon said in the House of Representatives that the speech given by Campbell, the British Consul-General in New York, at the banquet of the Women's International League for Peace and Freedom on April 17, attacking the Vinson Naval Bill, was suspected of interfering in U.S. internal affairs and should be recalled by the British government. Today, Campbell denied the accusation, saying that he accepted the invitation of the association but did not know that it was discussing the Vinson proposal. Several people who spoke before him did attack the bill, but he spoke solemnly and never mentioned the bill or any legislation in Congress. The Vinson Naval Bill provides for the United States to build warships to the limit allowed by the London Naval Treaty and stipulates an expenditure of 500 million yuan. The bill was signed into law by President Roosevelt on March 27 this year. (Reuters, 21st)

Goering Announces: Germany's Domestic and Foreign Policy, Domestically Stable, Unyielding Externally 36

(Berlin) Prussian Prime Minister and German Cabinet Aviation Minister General Goering received a Reuters interviewer today in his room, which was decorated with a swastika flag, and discussed German domestic and foreign affairs at length in a frank manner. Goering, dressed in a white flannel suit, smiled as he spoke, saying that he loved England very much, but he was often misunderstood by the English people. He regretted that the English newspapers had vilified him as a "bloodthirsty pig" and did not understand the reason for such slander. He pointed out that the British government, like the German government, had to approve the death penalty. People who kill will be killed, otherwise they will kill again. Since Germany reinstated the death penalty, the number of murder cases has greatly decreased. Goering then spoke about aircraft, saying that he did not have military aircraft, but he did not deny that he had requested them. The issue of German air defense would eventually be discussed. Some people still accuse Germany of secretly rearming, but do you think I can build an air force of 3,000 aircraft like France without being feared? Why bother harping on it? The whole world knows that France does not want to disarm, but if France wants war, then I can't do anything about it. However, all the people of Germany will rise up together to protect the German border when the country is invaded. Goering continued to talk about domestic affairs, saying that Germany's position was completely stable, but the government's procedures would take several years to implement effectively. Communism has been eradicated, but if this doctrine exists in other countries, it is still dangerous and cannot be eliminated. Other countries are very lenient in their treatment of communists in detention centers, so that the communists have become more active recently. In order to cope with this trend, I have decided to issue strict punitive measures. There are currently about six or seven thousand people in German detention centers, most of them communists. When asked whether communist leaders such as Thälmann could be released, Goering replied that there was no such question, because they were very disobedient and the charges against them were still in progress. Thälmann's life in prison is still good. He has abandoned communism and asked whether the government, which now has the support of 99% of the people, could be lenient with him. He (Goering) replied that this statement was very wrong. If 1% of the people in the country resist the government and are not stopped, then this 1% will start propaganda and bewitch the 99%. Propaganda is very harmful if it is not counteracted. (Reuters, 20th)

Paris Communist Party and Socialist Party Clash Violently with Police Again; Hold Mass Meeting to Oppose Government Salary Cuts; Over a Thousand Detained, Foreign Nationals to Be Deported 37

(Paris) Despite strict government bans on gatherings, the Communist and Socialist parties secretly planned to hold a mass meeting today on the Rue du Faubourg-Montmartre to oppose the order to cut civil servant salaries and to protest against the government and Fascism. However, the police, forewarned of their plan, took strict precautions. When demonstrators marched in a column to the square on that street, they were blocked by the police. A violent confrontation ensued. Thousands of police and patrolmen guarded each street entrance leading to the square. Seeing no way to reach their meeting place, the demonstrators initially lingered outside the restricted area, remaining relatively calm. But soon, their anger became uncontrollable, and they clashed with the police. The first clash occurred at 6:30 PM, presenting a comical scene. It was raining heavily, like a forest of umbrellas waving, and police and Communists slipped and fell on the road one after another, covered in mud. Shortly after, the scene resembled the riots of February. Large numbers of Communist Party members, Socialist Party members, and civil servants charged forward, attempting to reach the square, but were repeatedly repelled by the police. As the demonstrators attacked, they sang the Internationale loudly. Despite their best efforts, they failed to reach their destination. The police were very effective in suppressing the riot. Although several people were struck on the head during the fighting, no serious consequences occurred. Therefore, before midnight, half of the police present had withdrawn. Over a thousand demonstrators were arrested in the operation. Most will be released after questioning, but foreign nationals among them will be severely punished or deported. (Reuters, 20th)

(Paris) Tonight, two thousand disabled veterans of the European War marched through the bustling streets to protest against the recent government austerity measures, especially the order to reduce disability benefits. The demonstrators dispersed in front of the Place de l'Opéra without incident. (Havas, 20th)

(Paris) Six thousand people, responding to the call of the Communist Party and orthodox Socialist Party, held a demonstration in front of the City Hall Square, defying the Interior Ministry's ban. These people, united with civil servants, protested against the government's austerity measures and the disciplinary actions against postal and telecommunications workers. At 6:30 PM, when shops and factories closed for the day, clashes began between demonstrators and police. By 6:45 PM, the crowd in front of the City Hall Square had been dispersed by the police. Order was restored by 7:00 PM, and some police units withdrew. A total of 960 people were arrested, including some foreigners, all of whom will be deported. (Havas News Agency, 20th)

(Paris) Paris is again in a tense state today. Thousands of rioters gathered in the bustling streets, including Communists, Socialists, and veterans of the Great War. They marched through the streets to City Hall to petition for the immediate resignation of the entire City Council and the abolition of the Paris City Hall. This disturbance was triggered by Premier Doumergue's austerity policy, which aims to reduce expenditures by 2.56 billion francs. Most of those affected by the salary cuts are civil servants and veterans. The police made every effort to suppress the rioters and prevent them from entering the City Hall. About a thousand people were arrested, of whom 940 will be detained for one day and then released. Others carrying weapons will be charged with rebelling against the government. After several hours of suppression, order was restored by midnight. Premier Doumergue's attitude is extremely firm, refusing to rescind the austerity measures. He argues that there is no other way to alleviate the country's current difficulties; otherwise, the government's finances will be in dire straits, and all domestic and foreign debts will be defaulted. However, these austerity measures are temporary in nature, and everything will return to normal once the crisis has passed. (National News Agency, 20th)

French New Submarine Can Travel Half the Globe Without Refueling; Another Destructive Force Added to the Sea 38

(Paris) The French Navy's newest submarine, the "Suffren," is nearing completion, adding another destructive force to the ocean. According to reports, this new submarine has a displacement of 3,000 tons and a range of 12,000 miles. It can travel half the globe without refueling. The submarine is 360 feet long, with a surface speed of 20 knots and an underwater speed of 11 knots. Its armament includes 14 torpedoes, four 20-centimeter guns, six anti-aircraft guns, and it can also carry a small seaplane. The submarine will be launched on June 11. (National Telegraph, 20th)

Tea Merchants Petition the Ministry of Finance to Stop the Harsh Tax Collection in Anhui Province 44

(Nanjing) The Zhenjiang Tea Association in Nanjing City, Anhui authorities established a tea short-term business tax in disguise, which is similar to a likin tax. The original tax rate was 10 per thousand of the capital amount, but this year it has been increased to 15 per thousand, and the recruitment of merchants for bidding is more than twice that of the previous year, exceeding the tea likin tax amount during the warlord era. When new tea is on the market, merchants go to the mountains to purchase, but they do not know what to do because the tax rate has not been clearly defined. Therefore, the association elected nine representatives, including Chen Shisheng, Xiang Zhengwu, and Chen Yugeng, to go to the Ministry of Finance on the 21st to request that the tea short-term business tax collected by Anhui Province be stopped. Gao Peide, a section chief of the Taxation Department, received them. The representatives stated that the short-term business tax is a disguised tea likin tax, and the contractors set up checkpoints along the way, harming merchants and people, and severely impacting the only product of Anhui merchants. They asked to forward the report to the minister and telegraph to the subordinates to stop it. Gao agreed to forward it for review and handling. (Special Dispatch, 21st)

Japanese and Puppet Military Police Arrest Chinese and Russian Employees of the East China Railway 93

Suspected of Smuggling Large Quantities of Medicines and Medical Equipment 94

Russian Consul in Harbin Lodges a Strong Protest with the Puppet Manchukuo Government 95

Harbin dispatch, On the 12th of this month, Li Xizhen, the Chinese director of the Sanitation Department of the East China Railway Bureau, was arrested at his residence in Nangang by the Japanese Kempeitai in Harbin and detained in the Kempeitai headquarters. At noon on the same day, several senior Soviet staff members of the Sanitary Squad were also arrested one after another by Jiang Kou, the head of the Criminal Section of the Puppet Harbin Police Department, and puppet detectives. The reason for the arrest of Li and others was that the Central Railway Hospital in Nangang, Harbin, which is under the jurisdiction of the East China Railway Sanitation Department, had a stock of valuable medicines worth more than 500,000 gold rubles, along with valuable medical equipment worth more than 300,000 rubles. Recently, all of them were lost completely. After many days of investigation by the Japanese Kempeitai and the puppet state police, it was learned that the Soviet side had secretly transported them back to their country. Moreover, the secret transportation did not start this year, but since the autumn of last year, they had been secretly packed and transported out of the country through Manchuria and Suifenhe. Although the area was surrounded by Japanese border police of the puppet state, the Russians still managed to transport the goods out. After the Japanese discovered this, they believed that the Chinese director Li Xizhen was involved in this matter and was suspected of colluding with Russian personnel in embezzling public property, so he was arrested. The Japanese considered the case to be of great importance, and many Chinese employees of the East China Railway were implicated. The Japanese Kempeitai is conducting a secret investigation. Shi Yiwuciji, the Soviet Consul-General in Harbin, visited Shi Luben, the special envoy for Beiman affairs of the puppet government, that afternoon and lodged a strong protest, saying that Soviet railway personnel should not be arrested arbitrarily, causing disruption to official business. The puppet special envoy sophistically replied strongly. In the evening, Bandu, the Soviet Deputy Director of the East China Railway, also sent a protest letter to Li Shaogeng, the Director of the East China Railway of the puppet government, saying that the Japanese were obstructing railway affairs and the puppet state should not be instigated by them to arrest railway personnel. Li did not reply. The Russian Director, Ludi, also sent an official letter to Li Shaogeng, saying that the management and staff of the East China Railway no longer have legal protection and everyone is feeling the danger to themselves, which has a significant impact on the railway's operations. If this results in losses to the railway's business, the puppet Manchukuo side will be responsible. Li Shaogeng dared not reply without authorization and has telegraphed the Ministry of Transport of the puppet capital for instructions. After Li Xizhen was arrested, the puppet Director Li Shaogeng appointed Li Jimin, a special commissioner of the department, as acting director in his place, but the Russian Director Ludi refused to sign the approval and directly appointed Si Zhichiqi, a physician of the department's epidemic prevention, to act as director. The puppet side tried hard to argue but to no avail. Currently, both sides are doing their own thing. The Japanese side ordered the puppet Director Li Shaogeng to negotiate with the Russian side and demand the return of the stolen medicines, otherwise, it would summon certain senior officials of the East China Railway and investigate who was behind it, intending to intimidate them and retrieve the medicines and equipment, but the Russian side did not move. Li Xizhen is the son of Li Youlan, the former Liaoning Eastern Border Circuit Commissioner. Li Youlan and Yuan Jinkai co-founded the Puppet Fengtian Security Maintenance Association, but later, fearing public criticism, he fled into the pass. His son, however, continued to serve the puppet state outside the pass, and it was unexpected that he would be arrested by the Japanese now.

In addition, on the 11th of this month, eighteen freight cars of the East China Railway Harbin Station suddenly disappeared. The puppet side, on Japanese orders, investigated in detail for a long time and finally discovered that they had been secretly transported back to their country by Soviet railway personnel. The cars were also fully loaded with raw materials for the manufacture of munitions and poison gas collected from various parts of Northeast China. After the investigation was completed, Shi Luben, the special envoy for North Manchuria affairs of the puppet government, lodged a protest with the Russian consulate in Harbin, but the Russian side adhered to pragmatism and remained silent regardless of the protest. This, like the incident of the theft of medicines, is a serious unresolved issue. (13th)

Dai Chuanxian Passes Through Lanzhou to Qinghai 96

Accompanied by Yang Hucheng from Shaanxi to Lanzhou 97

Stays in Lanzhou for Three Days Before Flying to Qinghai Again 98

Also Visits Various Temples Along the Way 99

Lanzhou airmail dispatch, Dai Chuanxian, President of the Examination Yuan, Yang Hucheng, Director of the Xi'an Pacification Headquarters, and his wife, Xu Gongwu, Secretary-General of the Examination Yuan, Wang Yingyu, Deputy Chairman of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, Buck, a water conservancy consultant, and Lu Yuzheng, a civil engineer, and six others flew to Lanzhou from Shaanxi at 1:20 PM on the 12th. Li, the Secretary-General of the Gansu Provincial Government who went to Jiangxi to receive training, the Director of the Water Department, and Tan, the Director of the Qinghai Civil Affairs Department, also arrived in Lanzhou. After Dai and Yang got off the plane, they shook hands with each of the welcomers, then took a car into the city and stayed at the Provincial Government. In the future, he would do his best to work for the Northwest. Gansu is superior to other provinces in terms of heaven, earth, and people, but it lacks a 'doing' determination, so various constructions have not achieved much success. In the future, as long as we work hard, the future will be very smooth, because the Premier has planned everything for us, and we just need to follow the blueprint. In the future, a society of universal harmony will not be difficult to realize in the Northwest. Yang Hucheng and Deng Baoshan also gave speeches, and the words were all sincere. At 1:00 PM, they visited the Provincial Relief Institute, the Orphanage, and the Women's Normal School, and at 2:00 PM, they visited the Agricultural School and the Gansu Academy, and gave speeches to various secondary schools in Lanzhou at the Academy. At 5:00 PM, they attended the banquet of Party, military, and government officials. On the 15th, Dai took a plane to Qinghai again, accompanied by Xu Gongwu, Wang Yingyu, Buck, and Lu Yuzheng. The flight took off at 10:30 AM. Yang Hucheng, Zhu Shaoliang, Deng Baoshan, and others went to the airport to see them off. After Dai boarded the plane, the plane circled Lanzhou several times before flying west. Although it was only a few days in Lanzhou, the impression of various situations was very good. This is really a blessing for the future of Gansu. After I arrive in Qinghai today, I will rest for one night and visit Ta'er Temple tomorrow (the 16th), because that is a famous temple in Qinghai. I will tour that place for a day. I will return to Qinghai Provincial City on the 17th, give speeches to fellow countrymen from all walks of life, and visit various places. Because I am eager to return to Beijing to handle various affairs, I will not be able to stay in Qinghai for a long time, so I plan to take a direct flight to Xi'an on the 18th. On the 19th, I plan to go to Wugong with Chairman Shao of Shaanxi and others to attend the groundbreaking ceremony of the agricultural school. At the same time, Wugong is not far from Baoji. There is Baoji Gorge on the south bank of the Wei River in Baoji, which is very convenient for water conservancy. The Central Government plans to help the Shaanxi Provincial Government open a canal in that place. The amount of land that can be irrigated by this canal will exceed the Jinghui Canal. However, Shaanxi Province has financial difficulties and may not be able to host this independently. Therefore, the Central Government plans to co-host it with the Shaanxi Provincial Government in order to complete it as soon as possible. After the visit to that place is completed, I will go to Meishan to visit the agricultural farm attached to the agricultural school in that county, and I can return to Beijing on the 22nd or as late as the 23rd.

Wang Yingyu Talks About the Yellow River Management Plan 100

Wang Yingyu, Deputy Chairman of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, came to Gansu this time with Chairman Dai to investigate water conservancy and has now completed his work. He flew to Qinghai by special plane on the 15th. Before leaving, he met with reporters and said, "Chairman Dai paid close attention to water conservancy in the Northwest during this trip. Therefore, when departing from Beijing, he made a special appointment to travel with me to consult on water conservancy matters. After arriving in Gansu, according to investigations from all parties, I deeply feel that the construction of water conservancy in Gansu is also really urgent. After Chairman Song comes to Gansu for inspection, there will definitely be a whole plan. This Association will also do its best to help host it. However, the mission of this Association is water conservancy in the provinces along the Yellow River. If the Yellow River is not well managed, not only will water conservancy be out of the question, but the Yellow River floods in recent years will also be impossible to eliminate. Therefore, managing the Yellow River is the fundamental solution to water conservancy in Shanxi, Shaanxi, Gansu, Ningxia, Hebei, Shandong, and Henan. I (Wang refers to himself) feel that the Yellow River breaches every year, which is really a great disaster for all provinces. In the future, the management of the Yellow River will be carried out in three sections, that is, divided into three reaches, from Shaanxi to the west as the upper reaches, from Shaanxi to the east to the junction of Shandong and Henan as the middle reaches, and from western Shandong to the estuary as the lower reaches. Regarding the management methods for the upper reaches, it is planned to plant trees on both banks to consolidate the dikes and avoid breaches. At the same time, divert river water to the sandy fields on both banks of the Yellow River in order to use the force of the water to accumulate good soil and gradually turn the sandy fields into good land, which can not only help consolidate the dikes but also be used for cultivation and open up sources of profit. Regarding the middle reaches, the Liuyuankou and Heigangkou areas have often breached in recent years, and the provincial capital of Kaifeng is in great danger. The reason for this is that the Mangshan Mountain west of Luoyang is close to the river. The mountain is made of blunt soil, and the river water erodes it, causing a large amount of sand and soil to flow into the plains of the Heigangkou area, raising the riverbed in that area, so it is easy to breach. In the future, it is planned to build dikes on the west side of Mangshan Mountain to save this disaster. Regarding the lower reaches, every year in summer and autumn when the river water rises sharply, the Ljin area of Shandong often suffers from floods. The reason why that area often suffers from floods is that the river course in that area is uncertain, sometimes flowing east and sometimes flowing south. In the future, the management plans to deepen that area, build dikes on both banks, and divert the river course to the Litinjkou, where the river water can be easily discharged. If the river water is not easily discharged, breaches will naturally not occur again. If the Yellow River can be managed in this way, the water conservancy problems of several provinces will be easily solved." (April 18th)

Liu's Bandits Break Through 101

Fleeing Again into Jiangsu's Ganyu County 102

Zhan and Gu's Troops Enter Jiangsu to Pursue and Suppress Them 103

Jinan dispatch, After Liu Guitang's bandit troops were severely attacked by the bandit suppression army near Qishan, Anqiu, due to excessive casualties, they were no longer able to form a single force and fled in a panic towards Zhucheng and Jizhou. On the night of the 18th, they stopped and rested in the Shichang area, 60 li northeast of Juxian County. Upon receiving the report, Han Fuju, believing that the area was surrounded by mountains and the terrain was dangerous, mobilized a large army that night to encircle and suppress them in order to completely wipe them out. Unexpectedly, after midnight, heavy rain poured down, and Liu's bandits took advantage of the rain to break through the encirclement and flee south. At 9:00 AM this morning, they had reached the Yangjiaguan Village, 45 li southeast of Juxian County. The 81st Division of Zhan Shutang's troops rushed from the south of Juxian County to intercept them, killing more than 30 bandits, capturing more than 40, and seizing 18 horses, more than 20 rifles and carbines, and more than 70 rounds of ammunition. The bandits were defeated and fled in panic to the south, passing through Doushan River, Tengjia River, Wangjia Pit, Pan Dianzi, crossing Jiazi Mountain, passing through Zhu Juntang, Tushan, Qingfengyu, Xiaohushan, and Majiazhuang, and turning east. They fled east along the Xiuqian River through Luojiayu, Qian Yequ Shangzhuang, and Xiazhuang, and entered the border of Rizhao. They passed through Xiao'er Mountain, Deli Village, Shangshan Village, Dahuang, and Xiaopo Village, and arrived near Maxin Mountain at noon. The various bandit suppression troops continued to track and pursue them. At 4:00 PM, the bandits fled north again through Qianhou He Village to the vicinity of Shengguan Mountain. After being intercepted by Zhan Shutang's troops, they turned south again and crossed the mountains south of Dahekou Village to the Zhucao Village area. This area is the border between Shandong and Jiangsu and is the southwestern border of Rizhao County, only four or five li from the border of Ganyu County, Jiangsu. Because the army was pursuing them very closely, Liu's bandits fled again into Ganyu County, Jiangsu.

After Liu's bandits re-entered Jiangsu from Shandong, Han Fuju telegraphed Wang Jun, commander of the 7th Division, to send troops to intercept them. The bandit suppression army in Shandong Province continued to pursue and suppress them without regard to borders. According to Han Fuju's statement today (19th), Liu's bandits fled to the border between Jiangsu and Shandong, and he has sent Zhan Shutang's division, Tang Bangzhi's brigade, and Li Xuande's cavalry regiment to track and pursue them. He has also ordered Gu Liangmin's division of the 22nd Division to pursue them south from Linyi. According to the announcement of the Shandong Headquarters, (1) On the 17th, a company commander of Liu's bandits, Xue Ruitian, 30 bandits, five rifles and carbines, 25 rounds of ammunition, and three mules and donkeys were captured by the militia in Changle; (2) Cheng Shibiao, a lieutenant adjutant of Tang Bangzhi's brigade, killed 24 bandits and obtained 15 guns when pursuing and suppressing Liu's bandits near Qishan on the 17th, and was extremely brave; (3) On the 18th, the Yishui militia captured a bandit named Yang Zhilian, who admitted to serving as a quartermaster in Liu Guitang's troops and said that all the money looted in recent days had been abandoned because they were severely attacked by the army in Qishan on the 17th. (19th)

Guangdong Finance Department Borrows Funds to Maintain Paper Money 107

The Loan Amount Totals Five Million Yuan 108

Guangzhou dispatch, The Guangdong Finance Department has borrowed funds from the business community to maintain the paper money of the Provincial Bank. The loan matter has now been realized. In recent days, the price of paper money has risen from 90% to 95%. If the government continues to increase the reserve funds of the Provincial Bank, reduce the amount of paper money in circulation, and collect all county taxes in paper money, it will not be difficult for the price of paper money to return to its full value in the near future. The procedure for the Finance Department to borrow funds is to raise funds from two aspects. A loan of 1.5 million yuan was borrowed from the cigarette industry and was signed on the 10th of this month. 350,000 yuan was paid on the same day, and the remaining 1.15 million yuan will be paid in installments. This loan is allocated and borrowed by the cigarette industry according to the amount of unified tax paid by each tobacco company in the most recent three months. The Nanyang Tobacco Company borrowed 420,000 yuan, the British American Tobacco Company borrowed 310,000 yuan, the Dahua Company borrowed 200,000 yuan, the Guoxiang Tobacco Company borrowed 160,000 yuan, the Minzhong Tobacco Company borrowed 120,000 yuan, and other cigarette companies borrowed 290,000 yuan to make up 1.5 million yuan. The cigarette industry signed a contract with the Finance Department, stipulating a weekly interest rate of one percent and a loan term of eight months, with tobacco unified tax as collateral. If it is not repaid by the deadline, the cigarette merchants are allowed to deduct it from the tobacco unified tax payments. In addition, 3.5 million yuan is undertaken by a merchant named Huo, who guarantees it with a certain donation fund. Since the 12th, Huo has paid 1 million yuan in cash and 1.5 million yuan in provincial paper money, totaling 2.5 million yuan, to the Finance Department, which was then allocated by the Finance Department to the Provincial Bank as reserve funds. The remaining 1 million yuan is expected to be paid in full by around the 15th of this month. The Provincial Bank has been able to freely exchange cash for several days due to this large sum of cash, and the price of paper money should be able to restore its full value in a few more days. The government's plan to increase the agricultural product tax surcharge as a reserve fund for the Provincial Bank is also actively underway, and it is also preparing to issue special tax certificates for imported agricultural products for a short period of time. Merchants can first receive them in provincial currency and then use the certificates to offset tax payments in the future. The special tax bureaus for agricultural products in various places will handle this. (April 14th)

He was immediately sent to the hospital for treatment, and it is heard that there is a risk of a broken arm.

Pavilion Forest Town Neglectful Police Officer Xie Song to be Interrogated 110

Regarding the case of four bandits robbing a fisherman's family in Yuan Ye in East Street, Pavilion Forest Town on the evening of the 18th, and kidnapping relatives Wang and Yao, two girls, as previously reported, it is now known that the Wang girl is from Hougang, and the Yao girl is from the Zhangyan elite family. After the incident, the fisherman's wife Gu sneaked out to call the police to pursue the bandits. At that time, four police officers were only a few dozen steps away from the fleeing bandits. They saw the two hostages, one being carried and one being led, staggering away. However, the police neither fired a warning shot nor rushed forward to rescue them, but instead ran back to the station to gather their colleagues to chase them. The bandits had already gone far. Therefore, the Gu family reported that the four bandits only carried one broadsword, and the four police officers were fearful and unwilling to advance, failing in their duties. Yesterday, they specifically reported to Song for severe punishment. Director Zhou ordered Branch Director Yang Meilin to send the three negligent police officers to Song today for interrogation and, at the same time, send separate notices to the water and land police guard agencies to find ways to rescue the hostages.

Nanhui Fifth District Kidnapping Case Criminal Executed by Firing Squad 111

The home of Ju Xichang, a farmer in Dongxu Township, Fifth District, was robbed by bandits in December of last year, and his sons Xueming and Xuewen were kidnapped. Later, the detective team of Yuyao County, Zhejiang, arrested Wang Yueming (from Deqing Township, Yuyao) as the kidnapper in this case and rescued the two Ju sons who had been kidnapped. The county government then sent police to escort them to the case. After repeated interrogations, the criminal confessed to forming a gang to rob and kidnap people for ransom without denying it and was sentenced to death. This was submitted to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for approval. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, the county extracted the criminal Wang Yueming, verified his identity, and ordered the police team to escort him to the execution ground outside the South Gate for execution by firing squad.

Kunshan President Lin Inspects Prison and Justice 112

Lin Biao, President of the Jiangsu High Court, accompanied by a clerk, arrived in Kunshan by train from Suzhou on the afternoon of the 20th. After getting off the train, he went directly to the county government's local prison. The prison warden, Miao Wengui, had requested leave due to illness and went to Shanghai for medical treatment. Staff member Wang Lianyun presented various forms for inspection. He also accompanied President Lin to inspect the local prison and the male and female detention centers. President Lin praised the prison's hygiene and various facilities. County Magistrate Peng Baichuan and Judge Zhang Yizhi learned of his arrival and came to pay their respects. After a brief conversation, President Lin went to the county government to inspect the Justice Department and the courtrooms. After the inspection, County Magistrate Peng and Judge Zhang accompanied President Lin to Ma'anshan to visit various scenic spots. At 6:00 PM, President Lin took the Shanghai-Changzhou train to leave Kunshan and return to Suzhou.

Suzhou Money Shop Assistant Manager Missing 113

Zhou Dongqiu, assistant manager of the Yongge Money Shop in Tinglin Mountain Town, a county under Suzhou's jurisdiction, attended a friend's celebratory banquet the night before last (the 20th). He happily left at 11:00 PM, but on his way home near a small alley, three brawny men followed him. Zhou then went missing. The shop urgently sent people to search for him in all directions. As of 11:00 AM yesterday morning (the 21st), there was still no news. The incident was reported to the headquarters of the Sixth Water Police Team stationed in the town for investigation. It is said that when Zhou went missing, he had a diamond ring worth 2,000 yuan and banknotes on him. It seems that he was robbed and kidnapped.

New Life Movement Scheduled for Expanded Promotion

Since the New Life Movement in Wu County has been vigorously promoted by all sectors of society, it has been flourishing and has made a good impression. It has now been decided to convene various groups, organizations, and schools at the public stadium on May 1st to hold an expanded promotional meeting. The budget is set at 120 yuan, and the county party headquarters, the county government, and the county chamber of commerce are designated as the presidium. The conference is divided into three sections: general affairs, publicity, and discipline, with the county party headquarters and chamber of commerce responsible for general affairs, the county government's education bureau and farmers' association responsible for publicity, and the public security bureau and labor union responsible for discipline.

Jiading Performing Tan Huang, House Collapse Causes Death 114

The Taihe Tea House in front of the Huguo Temple outside the West Gate was opened by Pan Fushou, who borrowed the house from Changfeng Xinghang, and has been in business for many years. Because Pan's business was slow, he recently hired Wang Dongsheng from Taixing, his 16-year-old son, and his 12-year-old son to perform Tan Huang. The performances were very popular. Because the house had been in disrepair for many years, at 2:00 PM on the 20th, not long after the performance began, a central beam in the building suddenly came loose from the mortise joint where it was inserted into the pillar. The floor collapsed with a crash, and dozens of audience members fell down, suffering many injuries. An eight-year-old female student, Wang Weirou, who was a student in the first grade of Lianxi Elementary School and the young daughter of Wang Qiren, the owner of Wang Yongmao Tofu Shop, asked for leave from school due to a minor illness and went to the teahouse to get some boiled water. She had just taken the pot to her mouth when the building collapsed and crushed her underneath. Her head and left temple were crushed beyond recognition. She was sent to Cunren Hospital in the city, where President Xu Pingshu diagnosed that her brain matter was flowing out and she was bleeding from all orifices. He deemed that she could not be saved. She died at home around 5:00 PM. Local men Xu Axiao and Wang Wenfu were both injured in the legs, Li Qingyun was injured in the waist, Huang Zhiqing was injured in the foot, and Shi Ama, a boy from Kunshan who came to Jiading to sell firewood, was injured in the leg. Local women Chen Jinshi and Xu Lushi were both injured in the legs, Hong Mashi was injured in the waist, and Zhou Zhangshi dislocated her ankle. After being sent to the hospital for treatment, they were all able to return home and their lives were not in danger. Gu Hongqian, the patrol officer in charge of the First Public Security Substation, arrived at the scene after the accident and took care of the situation. Later, he detained Pan Fushou, Wang Dongsheng, Wang's son, Wang's son, and the waiter Shi Agou and prepared a document to send them to the County Public Security Bureau to be transferred to the County Government for interrogation.

Wuxi Opening Coffin and Steaming Bones to Examine Apprentice's Corpse 115

Li Baoyou, the owner of a barbershop in Lishe Town, the 15th district under the jurisdiction of the county, and his wife, Dai, beat their apprentice, Chen Youfu, to death on November 12th of last year. Recently, the deceased's father, Chen Jiafu, came to Wuxi and, with the approval of the County Court, transported the coffin to the city the day before yesterday and opened it for inspection in an empty grave outside the West Gate. Because the body was decomposed, it was changed to steaming the bones for examination yesterday (the 21st). At 8:30 AM yesterday, the acting prosecutor ordered two forensic officials, Wang and Liu, to take out the bones sealed in the box and place them on the table. First, Chen Jiafu was asked to taste the water in the pot to ask if anything else had been added. Chen replied that it was pure water. Then, the forensic officials placed the bones in the steamer to steam. Steaming was completed at 11:00 AM. The bones were taken out of the steamer. Forensic official Wang used clean water to wash the skull, forensic official Liu washed the finger and toe bones, and the earthworker washed the thigh bones. By 12:00 PM, all 365 bones of the whole body had been completely cleaned and placed on the table, arranged in a human form. The acting prosecutor ordered the deceased's father, Chen Jiafu, and the defendants Li Baoyou and Dai to stand beside the table. He then ordered forensic official Wang to first examine the skull in detail and scrape it with a bowl's edge. He found it to be white with no injuries. He then ordered the deceased's father, Chen Jiafu, to point out where the fatal wound of the deceased was, but Chen was stunned and speechless. Shi then ordered forensic official Wang to scrape and examine the twelfth rib from the left rib to the right rib, but there were also no injuries. Other arm bones and ribs were also examined, and there were no injuries. The examination was completed after about half an hour. The findings were reported to the acting prosecutor for review. The acting official confirmed that there was no error and that the death was due to illness before death. At this point, the deceased's father, Chen Jiafu, was summoned for questioning. The acting official said, "Now that the examination is complete and no injuries have been found, you have also seen it on the spot. Do you have anything to say now?" According to Chen's statement, "The cause of my son's death is said to be different by the villagers. Many say that he was beaten to death by the defendant, but I did not see it. Moreover, according to what was published in the Xibao, it was also said that he was beaten to death, so I filed a petition to seek justice." After reviewing the statement, the acting official ordered him to be taken into custody. Then, the head of the 83rd map, Qiang Ronghua, the head of the 226th map, Cai Zixian, and the head of the 227th map, Chen Zizhao, were summoned for questioning. They were also ordered to sign a statement that they witnessed the examination of the bones. Finally, the official ordered the bones to be sealed in a box and taken to the court for storage. The empty coffin was buried there. At 1:00 PM, the defendants and the bones were taken to the court for review.

Zhenjiang Public Security Bureau Rectifies House Numbers 116

The Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau believes that with the ever-changing construction of the provincial capital, there are occasional omissions in household registrations and house numbers, which should be investigated and rectified. Therefore, it has specially dispatched administrative staff from the bureau, along with household registration police from various branches, to conduct investigations separately. Any omissions and newly built houses that have not yet been assigned house numbers have been listed for compilation and application. It is reported that this work will be completed within three to five days. It is also reported that in order to facilitate travelers' inquiries about relatives and friends, the bureau has specially replaced the existing street and lane name plates and indicated the starting and ending numbers within the lane below the street name. It is reported that the investigation and production have begun, and it will be implemented as soon as it is completed.

Nantong Lvsi Suffers from Military Disaster, County Funds for Relief 117

Lvsi previously suffered from a military disaster caused by the Jiangsu Provincial Marine Guerrilla Team, which robbed and killed five merchants and civilians. After deliberation by local public groups, it was decided to provide relief. The county government submitted it to the province for approval. Now, instructions have been received that the province has financial difficulties and cannot allocate funds. The relief funds for this case should still be raised by the county.

Yao Port Jiang Bank Protects Against Collapse 118

The Jiang Bank area of Nantong's Yao Port has recently been collapsing more severely. The central government believes that before the Yangtze River is comprehensively dredged and managed, the local government should make efforts to maintain the status quo. The county government has now submitted a request to the Construction Department for approval to expedite the work of protecting against collapse.

Hangzhou Ji Zu Hall Reconstruction Completed 119

The Ji Buddha Ancestral Hall (namely Yunmu Well Hall) in Jingci Temple on Nanping Mountain in Hangzhou has been in disrepair for many years and is in a dilapidated state. Therefore, last year, the Shanghai Bodhi Dharma Assembly launched a fundraising campaign for reconstruction. Now the project has been completed. The completion ceremony is scheduled to be held on the morning of the 29th of this month (i.e., March 16th of the lunar calendar). During the pilgrimage season, it is expected that there will be a grand occasion at that time.

Huzhou Rape and Murder Case, Perpetrator Sentenced to Death 120

Jiang Zhu, the mistress of the Tianshunzhai Incense Shop in Dongzha, Nanxun, was raped and murdered by her lover, Zhu Aliu (namely Chu Anan), on the night of February 25th of this year out of jealousy. The perpetrator has been arrested by the Nanxun Public Security Bureau and transferred to the Wuxing Local Branch Court. Prosecutor Xiong has concluded the investigation and prosecuted him for murder and assault. After a detailed trial by Judge Wen, the final arguments were declared. Yesterday was the date of sentencing. At 2:00 PM, the judge ascended to the first courtroom, summoned the defendant to the case, and verified his name, age, place of origin, address, and occupation. He then stood up and read out the judgment: Zhu Aliu (namely Chu Anan) is sentenced to death for premeditated murder; for the crime of assault, he is sentenced to six months of imprisonment. The sentences will be combined and executed with the death penalty. After the sentence was pronounced, the defendant claimed that he did not accept it and may appeal.

International Commercial Telegraph

Reuter's Special Commercial Report on April 21st 121

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price The London gold price was quoted at 135 shillings and 8 pence today, an increase of 5 and a half pence compared to yesterday.

London Silver Bar The London silver market closed weak today. The spot price was quoted at 19 pence and 6875, a decrease of 1875. The futures price was 19 pence and 75, a decrease of 25. In the morning, the United States and China sold, and India bought.

New York Silver Bar The New York silver market opened weak due to the weakness in London. The sentiment was very uneven. Generally, people are paying attention to today's meeting between President Roosevelt and the silver faction legislators, and it is expected that the bulls will have some settlements, fearing that President Roosevelt will oppose the silver faction's plan. The forward opening price was reduced by 25 to 10 points compared to yesterday's closing price.

Bombay Silver Bar The Bombay silver market closed calmly today. The spot price was 54 rupees and 7 annas, a decrease of 7 annas. The futures prices also decreased by 7 annas.

Exchange Market 122

British-American The London foreign exchange market was still stable this morning. The British-American exchange rate opened at 5 yuan, 1 jiao, and 7 and a half fen, a decrease of 25 compared to yesterday's American-British exchange rate. It fluctuated slightly afterward. The closing price was 5 yuan, 1 jiao, 6 fen, and 875, a decrease of 625 compared to the opening price. Also, 1 US dollar is equivalent to 3 shillings, 10 pence, and 4328 British gold.

British-French Today in London, someone bought francs, causing the price to rise. The British-French exchange rate opened at 77 francs and 53, which was 18 pounds lower than yesterday. It continued to decline afterward, closing at 77 francs and 34, which was 19 pounds lower than the opening price.

American-British Today, the New York exchange rate for British currency opened at 5.17.0, a decrease of 75 compared to the previous day's closing price. There was no increase or decrease in the 23rd market. The fourth market rebounded by 25, to 5.17.25. The fifth market declined slightly, changing to 5.17.125. The sixth market increased again, remaining at 5.17.25.

American-French Today, the New York exchange rate for French currency opened at 6.6825, an increase of 15 compared to the previous day.

The Trend of Further Reduction in the Gold Content of the US Dollar A London dispatch on the 21st states that the recent weakness of the US dollar has attracted much attention. However, it should be noted that this weakness is not commensurate with the amount of transactions, because the transactions are not large. The downward trend of American goods has led people to expect that President Roosevelt may further reduce the gold content of the US dollar in order to raise prices. The French franc is now very close to the New York gold export price, but if the gold price of the US dollar is not reduced, the current exchange rate may not be sustainable, because the authorities may not be willing to allow gold to be shipped to Paris. Although President Roosevelt announced his opposition to the silver inflation bill, the silver faction in Congress has expressed serious opposition to his remarks.

Hongsheng Foreign Company also received a telegram from London stating that, according to the New York dispatch of the London Financial News, there are many rumors in New York that President Roosevelt will now reduce the gold content of the dollar, causing the prices of the pound and franc in the London market to be very firm. The franc is now gradually approaching the point of gold export. Operators in the foreign exchange market say that foreigners are withdrawing a lot of deposits, and American investors and speculators are vying to buy foreign securities.

Temporary Difficulty in Achieving British Stable Exchange Rate A London dispatch on the 21st states that the remarks made by Mr. Sader, Vice President of the Central Bank of the United States, at the annual meeting of the American Chamber of Commerce yesterday have drawn attention to the fluctuations in the exchange market. At that time, the Manchester Chamber of Commerce proposed a motion criticizing the premature stability measures, but it was immediately withdrawn because Sader did not approve of the motion. Sader said that the main crisis in Britain is the indefinite delay in stability, which forced the gold countries to abandon the gold standard. The excessively high exchange rate of the pound against the reference currency franc is a serious matter, because the nature of their exports is competitive with each other. However, the trade between Britain and the United States has more complementary elements than competitive ones.

The New York securities market opened today with a hesitant and watchful appearance, as it was heard that President Roosevelt was unwilling to proceed with the silver legislation bill during the current Congressional session. The opening was stable, with limited fluctuations and uncertain trends. Maintaining the market situation was the news of commercial recovery. The number of transactions in the first hour after the opening was 460,000 shares. The Hongsheng Foreign Company's report on the market prices of 15 types of New York securities (as of 10:45 AM) is listed below:

Local News

Wang Jingwei Came to Shanghai Yesterday for Medical Treatment, Visited Tang Youren and Song Ziwen and Returned to Nanjing That Evening. It is Said That No Decision Has Been Made on Opening Traffic and Postal Services. If There is a Solution, It Must First Be Made Public and Never Secret. 127

Wang Jingwei, President of the Executive Yuan, came to Shanghai from Nanjing yesterday morning to seek medical treatment for his old illness and to visit Foreign Vice Minister Tang Youren. He returned to Nanjing by night train that evening. Details are recorded below:

Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning 128

Wang originally planned to come to Shanghai last week to seek medical treatment for his old illness, but he postponed it because he failed to meet with Chairman Chiang and others in Nanchang. It was not until 7:00 AM yesterday that he came to Shanghai from Nanjing on a special train on the Nanjing-Shanghai Railway. After getting off at the Nanxiang Station, he took his own car and went straight to his private residence on West Pubashi Road to rest. In addition to his wife, Ms. Chen Bijun, and Vice Minister Zeng Zhongming of the Ministry of Railways, those who came to Shanghai with Wang yesterday morning also included Navy Minister Chen Shaokuan, Vice Minister Zou Lin of the Ministry of Finance, and Vice Minister Gan Naiguang of the Ministry of Interior, all of whom got off at the North Station.

Seeking Medical Treatment 129

After returning to his residence, Wang immediately invited German doctor Nore to his private residence at 8:20 AM to examine his old illness of diabetes. The examination lasted about half an hour. Doctor Nore took Wang's blood back to the hospital for testing. At around 10:00 AM, Wang took a car to Nore Hospital on Avenue Joffre to inspect the results of the blood test. Nore also prepared Western medicine for Wang's treatment. He did not leave the hospital until around 11:00 AM and returned to his residence for lunch.

Visiting Tang and Song Separately 130

Wang, accompanied by Vice Minister Zeng Zhongming of the Ministry of Railways, went to the private residence of Foreign Vice Minister Tang Youren on Gamston Road at 9:15 AM yesterday to visit Tang's illness and discuss recent diplomacy. He did not leave until after about an hour. Then, at 3:00 PM, he went to Qiqi Road to visit Song Ziwen, a Standing Committee member of the National Economic Commission. He left at 3:45 PM. It is said that the content of the talks between Wang and Song yesterday was mostly about the progress of all construction projects of the Economic Commission.

Wang's Remarks 131

Wang told visiting reporters yesterday that the central government has not yet made any decision on the issue of opening traffic and postal services, because the fundamental solution is still under careful consideration. If there are other appropriate solutions or a decision is made to negotiate in the future, it should first be made public to solicit the opinions of the people of the country before making a final decision. There will be no secret negotiations. As for the rumor that Chairman Huang has a solution to this problem, I have not heard of it. In short, it is said that there should be a way to open it if it can be opened, and there should be a way to deal with it if it cannot be opened. But everything needs to be studied. Regarding the unofficial statement issued by the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs, our Ministry of Foreign Affairs has also issued an unofficial statement in response. There is no need for another statement. Although other countries have not made any official statements on this move by Japan, public opinion is extremely indignant.

Returning to Nanjing That Evening 132

Wang, accompanied by his wife Ms. Chen Bijun, Vice Minister Zeng Zhongming, Secretary General of the Executive Yuan Chu Minyi, and others, took the night train from the North Station at 11:00 PM yesterday to return to Nanjing. Navy Minister Chen Shaokuan also traveled with them.

Representatives of the National Labor-Management Parties, Wang Zhisheng Sailed East Yesterday, Qian Chengxu Hired as Consultant 133

The 18th International Labor Conference will be held in Geneva this year. The Chinese government and both labor-management parties have sent representatives to attend. Government representative Li Pingheng and others had already sailed east on the 10th of this month. Management representative Wang Zhisheng stayed in Shanghai due to some matters and could not travel with them. As the conference date is approaching, Wang specifically bid farewell to all parties yesterday morning. At 3:00 PM yesterday, he left Shanghai on the French mail ship Zhen Nusha. Various groups and Wang's relatives and friends went to the pier to see him off. In order to facilitate Wang's business trip abroad, the management hired Qian Chengxu as a consultant to the management representative. After accepting the appointment, Qian went to Nanjing at 3:00 PM yesterday to ask the government to issue a passport for him to go abroad. He is scheduled to leave Shanghai on the 11th of next month.

Tang Erhe Returned to China Yesterday, Accompanied by Japanese Legislator Hata Momosaku 134

Tang Erhe, a member of the Beiping Political Reorganization Council, represented China's medical community at the 6th Oriental Medical Congress in Japan. Now that the congress is over, Tang, who had been staying in Japan for a month, arrived in Shanghai yesterday on the Japanese ship Nagasaki Maru with his son, Tang Gui. The Shanghai Municipal Government sent Wang Changchun to the pier to greet them. Upon landing, several Japanese reporters asked him about his experience in Japan. Tang said that this trip to the East was purely for attending the medical conference and that there were no other missions. He also said that after arriving in Shanghai, he still needed to meet with Mr. Huang Yingbai. Hata Momosaku, a legislator from the Japanese Seiyukai, who came to China on the same ship, came to China to meet with key government officials and to investigate the current situation in China.

Huang Fu Went to Hangzhou Yesterday Morning, Stayed in Hangzhou Briefly Before Going to Moganshan 135

Huang Fu, Chairman of the Beiping Political Committee, accompanied by his secretary and staff, took a train from the Fanhuangdu Station to Hangzhou at 8:07 AM yesterday. The Railway Bureau specially attached a special car. Huang Boqiao, Director of the Two Railway Bureaus, Shen Yi, Director of the Municipal Works Bureau, and Huang's relatives and friends went to the station to see him off. It is said that Wang Keming, Director of the Finance Department of the Committee, also went to Hangzhou on the same train. Huang will stay in Hangzhou for a few days and then go to Moganshan for a short period of recuperation after sweeping the graves.

Chairman Lin is Scheduled to Return to Nanjing This Morning 136

National Government Chairman Lin Sen came to Shanghai to take care of personal matters and seek medical treatment for his old illness. Now that the matter is over, he is scheduled to take the 8:00 AM train from the North Station to return to Nanjing this morning. The Railway Bureau has prepared a special car for his use.

Sun Ke Will Come to Shanghai This Morning 137

Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, left Nanjing last night and will arrive in Shanghai this morning.

Song Ziwen Changes Trip to Nanjing to Tonight, Diverts to Northwest for Inspections 138

National Economic Committee Standing Member Song Ziwen received Zhang Gongquan, General Manager of the Bank of China, at his private residence on Qiqi Road at 10:00 AM yesterday to discuss the construction of a banking corporation. The conversation lasted approximately half an hour before Zhang departed. Originally scheduled to depart last night, Song has changed his plans to take the night train to Nanjing tonight, from where he will divert to the Northwest for inspections. The matter of the banking corporation will be actively pursued after Song returns to Shanghai.

Italian Aviator Peinadi Performs Farewell Flight Yesterday Afternoon, Flying Up, Down, and Sideways Around the City Several Times Before Landing 139

According to the Fuxing Society, Italian aviator Peinadi came to Shanghai with Zhang Xueliang in February and has performed his flying skills in Shanghai several times. He once hosted Shanghai's press at the Cathay Hotel to explain his mission to assist China's civil aviation. It is now learned that Peinadi has completed his public duties in Shanghai and will soon return to his country. Yesterday, he performed one last aerial show over the city. At noon yesterday, Peinadi took off from Hongqiao Airport, performing side-flying, inverted flying, straight dives, and barrel rolls over the Bund area. The sound shook the roofs, and passersby stopped to watch. After about ten minutes, he flew back to Hongqiao Airport.

Hawke Flew to Hangzhou Yesterday; Condor Aircraft Returns to Normal Flight After Repairs 140

According to the Huadong News Agency, American aviator Hawke, while performing in Jiangxi a few days ago with a Condor aircraft, had his aircraft suffer minor damage when his assistant forgot to put down the landing gear during landing, causing the aircraft's belly to touch the ground. At the same time, one propeller also sustained considerable damage. Therefore, Hawke came to Shanghai from Hangzhou the day before yesterday. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, he carried a propeller and flew to Hangzhou from Hongqiao on a trainer aircraft. After making some minor repairs to the Condor aircraft, it resumed normal flight. The representative of the Intercontinental Aviation Corporation, Po Lei, did not accompany Hawke yesterday due to pressing business in Shanghai.

Exhibits for Chicago Exposition to Be Shipped on May 1st; Chinese Representatives to Accompany; Letter Sent to U.S. Consul for Verification 141

According to the Xinsheng News Agency, this year's Chicago Exposition has been decided to open early on the 26th of next month. The association for China's participation in the Chicago Exposition had only shipped one-third of the exhibits to Shanghai as of yesterday. Therefore, the shipment by the Hoover Mail Steamer on the 24th is likely to be postponed again. A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency visited the person in charge of the association yesterday, and the details are recorded below.

Increase in Exhibits 142

Last year, China participated with over 420 crates of exhibits, but many were related to culture and art, with very few of an international trade nature. Although not all exhibits have arrived in Shanghai this year, there will be a strong increase of one-half compared to last year, totaling about 1,000 crates. Items such as porcelain, tea, and carpets are unique products of our country. It is hoped that their display in the United States will reverse the disastrous decline of our overseas market.

Shipping Date 143

Originally scheduled to be shipped from Shanghai on the 17th of this month, it was postponed to the 24th due to the exhibits not arriving in time. However, as of today, only one-third of the exhibits have been shipped to Shanghai, and they will definitely not be fully assembled by then. Therefore, the association sent a letter and telegram yesterday to Dong Fanfan and other locations, urging them to arrive by the end of this month. The final shipping date is set for May 1st on the President Grant steamer to Chicago. Chinese representatives accompanying the exhibits will include Dong Kunfan, Zhou Guanhong, and Zhang Wendi.

Customs Duties on Exhibits 144

The association sent a telegram to the Ministry of Industry yesterday, stating: "To Minister Chen of the Ministry of Industry: This association shipped a total of 420 crates of exhibits to Chicago last year. With your ministry's approval, the Ministry of Finance was consulted, and the Jianghai Customs Commissioner was instructed to collect taxes on the actual number of items sold and requested the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce to provide a guarantee. Now that the Chicago Exposition has decided to continue the exhibition this year, all the exhibits shipped by this association in the past will remain on display. We hereby request your ministry to review and approve, and kindly inform the Ministry of Finance to instruct the Customs Administration to instruct the Jianghai Customs Commissioner to allow the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce to guarantee the exhibits shipped to Chicago last year and to collect taxes on the actual number of items sold at the close of this year's conference to facilitate settlement."

Notification to the U.S. Consul 145

According to the Xinxin News Agency, the Association for China's Participation in the Chicago Exposition sent a letter to the U.S. Consul General in Shanghai yesterday, stating: "To the Consul General of the United States in Shanghai: This association has decided to continue participating in the 1934 Chicago Exposition at your country's invitation, adhering to the principle of good relations between our nations. This has been approved by our Ministry of Industry and communicated to your country's Chicago Exposition authorities through the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. In addition to collecting exhibits for display, we have appointed Zhang Wendi, Dong Kunfan, and Zhou Guanhong, standing directors of this association, to represent this association at the exhibition site and oversee the affairs of the Chinese pavilion. A list of accompanying personnel is attached separately. We hereby notify you for your reference. Respectfully submitted to Kirk Silverhelt, Consul General of the United States in Shanghai. Eurasia Aviation Corporation Purchases Latest Giant Aircraft; Interior Includes Kitchen and Can Carry 30 Passengers; Shanghai-Guangzhou (Over 2,000 Kilometers) Can Be Reached in One Day; Engineer He En Departed Yesterday by Plane for Inspection; Long-Distance Sino-German Air Route Expected to Be Realized Around June 146

According to the Huadong News Agency, Eurasia Aviation Corporation recently decided to purchase the German Junkers Ju 52 all-metal aircraft. The purchase of this latest aircraft is closely related to Eurasia Aviation Corporation's recently expanded route plans. In addition to maintaining the existing flight plans from Shanghai via Nanjing, Luoyang, and Xi'an to Lanzhou, with flights in each direction once a week, the company will also open new routes from Luoyang via Hankou and Changsha to Guangzhou and from Luoyang via Taiyuan to Beiping starting May 1st. These routes will connect in Luoyang, forming a direct air route from Beiping to Guangzhou. To enhance passenger comfort and shorten travel time on this route, the company purchased new aircraft. The aircraft can carry 30 passengers, and it only takes eight hours to travel from Beiping to Guangzhou. It is reported that this is the first time China has used this type of aircraft. The company also announced yesterday that the aircraft will arrive in Shanghai soon, and the Beiping-Guangzhou route and the Sino-German route to Xinjiang will use this aircraft for flights in the future. Engineer He En was dispatched yesterday to inspect the Beiping-Guangzhou route, so that flights can begin on May 1st. The Shanghai-Xinjiang route is expected to be realized in June this year. The details are recorded below.

Dispatching Personnel to Inspect the Beiping-Guangzhou Air Route 147

The newly opened Beiping-Guangzhou air route, recently established by the company, has been decided to commence operations on May 1st. The company has dispatched engineer He En yesterday to inspect the route. In the initial phase of operations starting on May 1st, the old aircraft will still be used. Once the new aircraft arrives in Shanghai, it will be replaced. The new aircraft is the Ju 52 type, measuring 19 meters in length, 6 meters in height, and 30 meters in width. The aircraft is equipped with complete radio communication equipment and direction-finding instruments, so it can determine the location of each station and the aircraft itself during flight, even without the assistance of ground radio stations, thereby enhancing flight safety. The aircraft's radio station is connected to the pilot's seat, allowing the pilot to calmly calculate the aircraft's location even during foggy conditions. The seats in the cabin are leather and extremely comfortable, and the view is very clear, allowing passengers to enjoy the scenery on both sides. The aircraft also has an electric kitchen, allowing passengers to eat comfortably. A distance of 2,000 kilometers can be reached in less than eight hours of flight if there are no intermediate landings.

Sino-German Flights Will Also Use New Aircraft 148

Eurasia Aviation Corporation plans to use the Ju 52 aircraft for the Shanghai-Lanzhou air route after the Beiping-Guangzhou route achieves good business results. This route is the first segment of the route from Shanghai via Dihua to the Sino-Russian border. Once the Ju 52 aircraft is used, direct air travel from Dihua to Europe will be even more convenient. The route from Lanzhou to Dihua is currently suspended due to unrest in Xinjiang. It is hoped that it can be resumed this summer. Eurasia Aviation Corporation is taking this opportunity to upgrade all flight equipment to provide the latest air travel conveniences to long-distance passengers when the Xinjiang route is resumed.

Largest Honor Awarded in Swiss Competition 149

The company announced yesterday that the new aircraft it purchased is excellent. The Junkers Ju 52 aircraft won the highest honor in the Alpine Aviation Competition held in Switzerland a few years ago. At that time, all the participants in the competition were transport aircraft. The main requirements were not only to have excellent flight capabilities but also to fly over the most difficult terrain in Europe, crossing mountain ranges of 4,000 meters. During the competition, the weather was extremely bad, and the aircraft had to fly in fog for several hours. The Junkers Ju 52 aircraft demonstrated its various advantages in this environment and won the greatest victory. The latest aircraft manufactured by the factory recently does not increase the horsepower but does increase the aircraft's power considerably.

Wing Particularly Suitable for China 150

The company also announced the advantages of the new giant aircraft's wings, stating that the Junkers auxiliary wing is installed at the rear of the wing and is equal in length to the wing. In calm winds, even when fully loaded with 3,500 kilograms, it only needs to travel 270 meters on the ground to take off. After taking off, the speed in the air can be increased to 260 kilometers per hour or even 300 kilometers per hour with the aid of this auxiliary wing. During landing, the aircraft's speed can also be reduced to only 65 kilometers per hour. Therefore, even when fully loaded with 3,500 kilograms, the Ju 52 aircraft only needs to continue for 180 meters on the ground after the wheels touch down to come to a complete stop. This aircraft is most suitable for use in China, where there are no extensive standby airport facilities along the route.
