Shanghai Machine-Made National Goods Industries Association Submits Document to the Executive Yuan Regarding Trademark Sound and Meaning 161

The Shanghai Machine-Made National Goods Industries Association submitted a document to the Legislative Yuan and the Ministry of Industry yesterday regarding the impact of the interpretation of trademark law on sound and meaning, stating: "Regarding the interpretation of trademark law, which presents an exception that harms national credibility, requesting (the Legislative Yuan) to propose supplements: According to the text of Article 1, Paragraph 2 of the Trademark Law, text, graphics, and symbols are inherently three different types. If the text does not contain sound and meaning, it is no different from graphics and symbols. Why must text be a prerequisite? This shows that text must contain sound and meaning. The difference between literate and illiterate people lies in whether they can read the sound of the word. If a deaf-mute person wants to be tested on whether they know a word or not, they must write another word with the same sound to show them. This is naturally the case. When illiterate people buy and sell goods, it depends entirely on what they hear and say. If trademark registration is permitted for trademarks with the same sound but different characters, wouldn't that encourage confusion? This has not been permitted by the Trademark Bureau's practice. However, since the Executive Yuan requested the Judicial Yuan's interpretation, it has been said that text does not contain meaning and is treated like graphics and symbols in general. This will allow cunning individuals to compete to use trademarks with the same sound but different characters to deceive the public, affecting the future of industry and commerce and overturning trademark precedents. The dignity of trademark registration will fundamentally disappear. Whether internally or externally, it is sufficient to harm national credibility. The only way to address this is to request your Yuan (your department to request the Legislative Yuan) to supplement Articles 1 and 2 of the Trademark Law based on the spirit of legislation, so as to reassure people and prevent cunning practices. As far as Article 1, Paragraph 2 is concerned, the original meaning is very broad and does not need to explicitly state that text includes sound and meaning. Because no one else has registered it before, there is no such thing as being the same or similar. Therefore, the crackdown is listed in the clauses of Article 2. The original intent of the legislation is very appropriate. However, for 'specified color to be applied,' it is proposed to add the word 'able' after the word 'parallel.' As for the original regulations, only one color is clearly applied, or there is no color at all, such as on glass bottles and iron lids. If imitators take different colors, they can argue. If the original registrant needs to prevent its disadvantages, they must first register all similar trademarks of various colors, which would result in a large income for the Trademark Bureau, but the industrialists and merchants could not bear the burden and it is also impossible to prevent. Therefore, if the word 'able' is added, those that are not necessarily similar are already included in the list of routine crackdowns. This is a request for Article 1, Paragraph 2. After listing the clauses in Article 2, it is proposed to add a clause: 'The aforementioned similarity or approximation includes the shape, color, sound, and meaning of text, graphics, and symbols. Anyone with a hint of imitation is included.' Because the trademark law has no clear provisions on the definition of approximation or similarity, this is a major shortcoming. As a result, the same case has different results, contradicting each other, making people unable to adapt. If it is clearly stipulated, it will be sufficient to prevent cunning and avoid various disputes. Therefore, we submit this document to request your Yuan (your department to request the Legislative Yuan) to adopt it, and contribute a foolish opinion. I can't help but look forward to it. Respectfully submitted to the Legislative Yuan of the National Government, Ministry of Industry."

Comparison of New and Old Tariffs on Imported Match Raw Materials 162

The Industries Association Forwards to the National Tariff Commission for Consideration

Foreign-made match raw materials are lightly taxed and dumped on the market, severely impacting domestic goods. The Shanghai Machine-Made National Goods Industries Association previously requested the National Tariff Commission to increase import taxes on foreign goods and reduce export taxes on domestic goods to demonstrate promotion. Yesterday, the association re-submitted a comparison of new and old taxes to the commission. The details are as follows:

Letter to the Industries Association 163

Huachang and other wood slice factories sent a letter to the Industries Association, stating: "We have found that poplar and American poplar are used as raw materials for match stems, boxes, and slices. They are soft and not suitable for building materials, but they are suitable for manufacturing stems and slices. This is well known in the wood industry. If they are left for half a year, the wood will rot and turn black, becoming waste. This should be exempted from tariffs to maintain the industry. In Japan, manufacturers of stems and slices do not pay taxes on imported poplar raw materials, and exports of semi-finished products are tax-free. When they are transported to our country, they only pay import tax once and can be sold nationwide. This is not the case for domestic products. They are taxed on imported raw materials and semi-finished products, and the taxes are unusually high, making it impossible to compete with foreign goods. Before the tax was added last year, imported raw materials cost 6.78 yuan per thousand square feet, including surcharges. After the new tax was imposed, the same thousand feet of wood now cost 12 yuan in import tax. White poplar is a domestic product and originally had no tax rate. Since the loss of the northeastern provinces four years ago, the Shanghai Customs has gradually increased taxes on goods from the Northeast, almost to the same level as foreign goods. In addition, the export tax on domestic semi-finished products was valued at 3.5 taels of customs silver per dan before the tax was added. After the new tariff was set, it suddenly increased by half, with each dan assessed at 7 taels of customs silver. With a 7.5% tax, each package of 189 catties of stems and branches must be taxed at 1.5 yuan. Foreign semi-finished products are also estimated by weight. In Japan, to reduce evasion, each package weighs only 160 to 170 catties, so the tax is only around 1.4 yuan. The same package of stems and branches is taxed at 0.15 yuan more. Adding the import tax on raw materials, each package must bear 2 yuan more, which is 2.15 yuan more than imported semi-finished products. Therefore, foreign goods rely on tax-free imports and exports to our country, paying tax only once and dumping at low prices everywhere. Domestic products are under pressure and are declining. Inventory is piling up, and the trend of stagnation is imminent. The previous letter detailed the process and was presented to the Ministry of Finance and the National Tariff Commission for their consideration. The comparison of the old and new tax rates and the two copies of poplar raw materials are enclosed. We urge your association to provide relief and appeal again to the National Tariff Commission for prompt approval to increase taxes on semi-finished products, exempt poplar raw materials from import tax, and reduce export tax on domestic stems, boxes, and slices, so that the national treasury will not be damaged, and the thousands of workers in this industry and the tens of thousands of people who indirectly rely on it for a living will be spared from unemployment. This is a gift from your association. The national economy and people's livelihood are of great importance. With the utmost urgency, we submit our respects."

Submission to the National Tariff Commission 164

The Industries Association submitted a document to the National Tariff Commission, stating:

"Regarding the submission of supplementary reasons to approve the reduction of tax rates: On April 7th of this year, member Huachang Stem and Slicing Factory and others jointly requested the government to reduce the export tax on semi-finished stems, boxes, and slices and the import tax on poplar raw materials, and to increase the import tax on foreign semi-finished products in order to replenish the national treasury and protect industry. Recently, the factory and others sent a letter stating (see above for details). Poplar and American poplar can only be used to manufacture stems and cannot be used as building materials and are also prone to rot, as stated above. The domestic overproduction and the intrusion of foreign goods have been stated in the previous submission. However, the comparison of the new and old tax rates was omitted. It is appropriate to supplement the document and use it as a reason to request a tax reduction. We humbly request your consideration and prompt action to classify building materials and stem materials separately to reduce the tax rate on stems and avoid industrial stagnation and worker unemployment. We await your urgent orders. The association also listed the comparison of new and old tariffs: (1) Import raw material tax: before the tax was added, poplar cost 6.78 yuan per thousand square feet, including surcharges; after the new tariff was set, poplar cost 12 yuan per thousand square feet, including surcharges. (2) Export tax on domestic semi-finished stems: before the tax was added, each dan was valued at 3.5 taels of customs silver, and each package of 190 catties was valued at 10.036 yuan, with a 7.5% tax of 0.777 yuan. After the new tariff was set, each dan was valued at 7 taels of customs silver, and each package of 190 catties was valued at 20.073 yuan, with a 7.5% tax of 1.5 yuan. (3) Import tax on foreign semi-finished stems: after the new tariff was set, each dan was valued at 7 taels of customs silver, and each package of 170 catties was valued at 18.54 yuan, with a 7.5% tax of 1.39 yuan."

Following the wave of strikes at the Mei Ya Silk Factory, and after the Party and government issued a notice ordering a return to work, all workers at the main factory complied. Rickshaw Pullers' Representatives Submit Letter to the Municipal Council, Requesting Strict Crackdown on Arbitrary License Confiscation 168

Chen Guoliang and others, representatives of Shanghai rickshaw pullers, yesterday submitted a letter to Mr. Zhong Siyun, Director-General of the Public Concession Municipal Council, regarding the issue of license confiscation, which has recently become increasingly severe, causing unbearable suffering for rickshaw pullers. They requested improved treatment for relief. The letter stated that rickshaw pullers rely solely on pulling rickshaws for a living, and once their licenses are confiscated, they are forced to stop working. Not only is the rickshaw rent not reduced, but they are also questioned by rickshaw owners and foremen. Rickshaw pullers are not careful, leading to various disputes and causing endless impact on their livelihoods. This is all due to the Municipal Council's license confiscation policy. However, regarding whether a license should be confiscated, according to numerous rickshaw pullers, in the past, there was a set time for confiscations, but now, regardless of the time of day, police officers are seen patrolling and confiscating licenses even after 10 PM, even when the quota for confiscations has been met. They disregard the livelihood of the weak nation's rickshaw pullers and deliberately oppress them, confiscating licenses at every opportunity. Furthermore, in the past, licenses could be retrieved immediately after confiscation, but now, it takes three to four days, six to seven days, or even more than ten days to retrieve them, with deliberate obstruction. Rickshaw pullers suffer every day they cannot work. Recently, the arbitrary confiscation of licenses by the police officers has harmed the livelihoods of rickshaw pullers, and so on. Representatives were moved to tears upon hearing this. Recalling that rickshaw pullers come to Shanghai to make a living due to rural bankruptcy, they lack capital for trade and have no one to help them find work, so they have no choice but to pull rickshaws, which is a difficult and laborious task, deserving of pity. The police officers arbitrarily confiscate licenses and arbitrarily fine rickshaw pullers' hard-earned money, and also delay their working hours, causing them various hardships. The association has repeatedly petitioned the Municipal Council Director-General to crack down on this issue. Since October of last year, upon receiving the Municipal Council's Rickshaw Committee's proposal on improving the rickshaw industry, the committee has prioritized the relief of rickshaw pullers. However, since then, not only has there been no improvement in the treatment and relief of rickshaw pullers, but the police officers' means of confiscating licenses have become even more severe. It is questionable whether this aligns with the original intention of relieving rickshaw pullers, and whether such a quota for license confiscations is legal. Recently, it has been found that at least hundreds of licenses are confiscated every day, and the period of confiscation has been extended. On average, the number of unemployed rickshaw pullers is alarming. If this continues, the unemployed rickshaw pullers, especially those with families, will inevitably starve and resort to desperate measures. Regarding the issue of license confiscation, the following improvements in treatment are requested: (1) If there are no damages or defects in the rickshaw, please do not be overly critical and arbitrarily confiscate the license, to avoid losses to the rickshaw pullers; (2) If the rickshaw needs to be confiscated, please repair it immediately and return it upon inspection, without detaining it and delaying working hours, to avoid hindering the rickshaw pullers' livelihoods; (3) Please allow rickshaw pullers to carry luggage, trunks, and other items, in addition to removing iron and wooden objects and items that hinder hygiene, to maintain their business. Therefore, they earnestly request the Director-General to review the above situation, treat the impoverished rickshaw pullers with compassion, and order the Traffic Department to strictly crack down on the arbitrary confiscation of licenses by the police officers and the harsh fines imposed on rickshaw pullers' hard-earned money. They would be extremely grateful and eagerly await orders.

The Preliminary Announcement of Yuan Yi Bank's Opening: The Realization of a Brand-New Financial Enterprise; A Tool for the Development of Industry and Commerce 171

Shanghai is the center of finance and commerce in the country, a metropolis where talents converge. All economic facilities and the development of industrial and commercial enterprises nationwide are based in Shanghai. Preparations for design, fundraising, and material procurement are completed in Shanghai before being carried out in various regions in sequence. Therefore, various economic organizations and material equipment are relatively complete in Shanghai. However, compared to advanced countries in Europe and America, they are still far behind. Large-scale and high-asset businesses, such as finance, trade, and insurance, are controlled by foreigners. Domestic investors who wish to invest in emerging businesses have no way to do so. If they entrust foreigners to manage their businesses, they will have to watch foreign stewards reap profits. As General Sun Yat-sen estimated, China loses an unknown number of tens of thousands of yuan each year due to foreign exchange transactions. In recent years, domestic investors have been able to work harder in new businesses, and have been able to recover some rights. In recent years, domestic investors have been paying increasing attention to investments in foreign securities and goods transactions. However, this enterprise is absolutely controlled by foreigners, and domestic investors cannot step beyond the bounds. A few months ago, it was heard that financial giants in Shanghai were planning to establish such an enterprise. Recently, it was learned that the purpose of Shao Changchun and Ge Zheisheng's trip to Europe and America was indeed for this matter. According to reliable sources, Yuan Yi Bank, organized by Hua Shang giants Wang Boyuan, He Gusheng, Liang Chenlan, Qi Shaozhai, Wang Zisong, Shao Changchun, Ge Zheisheng, and others, who raised huge amounts of capital and united the financial community, is almost ready and will open soon. The capital and scale of the bank are very large, with one million yuan already raised, and it is of unlimited nature. The scope of its business is extremely broad, handling all kinds of domestic and foreign government bonds, securities, and goods transactions, and providing agency services for buying and selling, which is especially welcome. The reason why Mr. Wang and others are willing to invest huge amounts of capital, overcome difficulties, and boldly decide to establish this business, despite the competition from foreign merchants, is that they have reached a proper agreement with the New York Chinese Chamber of Commerce's well-known cotton yarn, wheat, securities, and commodities exchange, as well as the Chicago Board of Trade. They have also specially appointed Mr. Mund, a giant in the New York securities industry, as their agent. At the same time, Shao and Ge competed for the position and negotiated in New York, and finally won the election as brokers. This is truly an unprecedented honor for Chinese merchants. Shao and Ge have already obtained the positions of brokers in the New York Cotton Exchange, the New York Commodities Exchange, and the Chicago Board of Trade. This is truly a groundbreaking feat for the Chinese business community, and the international commercial credit standing will be increased from now on. In the past, transactions had to go through Japanese or other foreign hands, but now Yuan Yi Bank can directly trade with foreign countries. Therefore, the establishment of Yuan Yi Bank not only adds a brand-new financial enterprise domestically, but also adds a lot of glory to the international position. The development and growth of Yuan Yi Bank should be celebrated by the Chinese people. It is hoped that national business leaders will work together and support each other to reverse the trend and consolidate the foundation of domestic commerce. It is understood that all the preparations for the bank are almost complete, and it will be officially opened in a short period of time. From now on, it will be a unique presence in the financial community, benefiting both the national economy and the people's livelihood. All of this is due to the efforts of Mr. Wang, Shao, and Ge.

Inspection Reports of Two Banks 176

The 194th Inspection Report on the Issuance Reserve of the Central Bank stated that, in accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, the committee is responsible for inspecting the reserve for the issuance of convertible notes of the Bank. The 194th inspection was conducted at the Issuance Bureau of the Bank on April 20, 1934, and the results are announced as follows: (A) The total amount of convertible notes issued was 67,939,191 silver dollars, including 61,538,990 silver dollar notes and 6,400,201 subsidiary coin notes. The total amount of the reserve for the issuance of convertible notes was 67,939,191 silver dollars, including 55,023,191 silver dollars in cash reserve. The cash reserve was 51,568,990 silver dollars in the Bank's issuance vault, 1,658,317 silver dollars in branches in various cities, and 1,795,884 silver dollars in other banks. The security reserve was equivalent to 12,916,000 silver dollars. (B) The total amount of customs gold convertible notes issued was 373,324.70 yuan. The total amount of the reserve for customs gold convertible notes was 373,324.70 yuan, including 7,351.95 taels of bullion, equivalent to 373,324.70 yuan of customs gold at a fixed price of 5.0779. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank's Regulations on Convertible Notes, the cash reserve should be 60% and the security reserve should be 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the security reserve is less than 40%, which is consistent with the regulations. This report is made on April 21, 1934, by Li Fuxun, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank, and Supervisors Xie Mingxun, Bei Songsun, Qin Lanqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, and Xu Jiliu.

The results are listed as follows: The amount of convertible notes in circulation was 37,572,469 yuan. The total amount of the reserve was 37,572,469 yuan, including a cash reserve of 29,081,629 yuan and a security reserve of 8,490,840 yuan.

According to the Far East News Agency, the Panchen Lama went to Hangzhou to initiate the Kalachakra Tantra Dharma Assembly. Special envoys were dispatched to Bailing Temple to invite more than thirty chanting Lamas. The first batch of five Lamas had already transferred from Beijing to Hangzhou for preparations. Yesterday, the second batch of Lamas and followers of the Panchen Lama, totaling more than fifty people, arrived at 8 AM on the Beijing-Shanghai through train from Beijing, with one first-class special carriage, one third-class carriage, and one baggage car. Chen Zhongxin, a 26-year-old Cantonese Catholic residing on the upper floor of Huaan Western Restaurant, Door No. 2, Wufeng Lane, at the intersection of Rue Joffre and Rue Massenet, French Concession, was the son of Chen Daxi, also known as Chen Youle, a 60-year-old prominent overseas Chinese businessman from Nanyang who owned a vast cocoa plantation in Rabaul. Chen graduated from the engineering department of the University of Bristol in England and qualified as an engine engineer. Injured in the Back of the Head 180

After being killed, the murderer, in an attempt to destroy the body, eliminate traces of the crime, wrapped all the quilts and clothes around the corpse, poured kerosene, and set it on fire. The murderer then took the opportunity to escape. It was discovered by the sub-landlord and waiter Chen Nianru. They initially thought that the tenant had gone out and that a fire had broken out in the room due to carelessness, and reported it to the fire department, who rushed to extinguish the fire. Pirate Leader Xu Xiaomei Arrested; Xu Robbed the Taizhou Ship; Arrested a Year After Incident 188

The Taizhou, a ship belonging to the Taizhou Shipping Company at No. 310 Magong Road, outside Guan Bridge in the Nanshi District, usually travels between Shanghai, Taizhou, and Haimen. In early May of the lunar calendar last year, the ship departed from Shen and set sail for Taizhou. Unexpectedly, at around nine o'clock that evening, while traveling five li from Haimen, a well-known pirate leader, Xu Xiaomei, along with dozens of accomplices, arrived in pirate ships, boarded the ship, ordered it to stop, and began a robbery. The crew and passengers on board were robbed, suffering significant losses. The pirates then loaded the stolen goods onto their pirate ships and fled without a trace. Afterwards, the ship owner reported the incident to the Haimen County government for investigation. However, nearly a year has passed, and the case remains unsolved. Unexpectedly, the pirate leader Xu Xiaomei, disguised as a merchant, boarded the ship in Shanghai yesterday, mixing with the passengers heading to Haimen, intending to commit further crimes. Fortunately, a tea server on board discovered her and secretly reported to the escort team, who immediately arrested Xu and sent her to the Haimen County government for severe punishment.

Creditors Like Wolves and Tigers, Jia Zhentang Commits Suicide; Miserable Poor Man, Creditors Violate Humanity 189

Jia Zhentang, a 48-year-old Shaoxing native living at No. 4 Luyanqing Lane, Muddy Beach Police Station, Pudong, was a small vendor. He had a son named Jia Rongquan, 21 years old, who worked in a cigarette factory, but his income was meager and barely sufficient for his own needs. The family was poor and had many mouths to feed, leading to frequent financial difficulties. In recent years, they had incurred further expenses for weddings and funerals, resulting in debts of over one hundred yuan to three or four creditors. Despite paying high interest rates, they were unable to repay the principal. Now, facing pressure from creditors, Jia, who had difficulty saving even from his food expenses to pay the interest, was unable to repay the principal immediately. However, the iron-faced creditors, like wolves and tigers, relentlessly pressured the poor man, making it impossible for Jia to cope. In a moment of desperation, he secretly bought a large amount of poison, likely opium, and committed suicide. He groaned and bled, and the poison had already penetrated deeply. He refused to tell his family, but his family, noticing his sudden and strange illness, realized he had taken poison and rushed him to Pudong Hospital for treatment. However, due to the depth of the poison and the passage of time, and because the poor family lacked the resources to transfer him to a more expensive hospital in Puxi, he died that night. His family still doesn't know what kind of poison he ingested. The Third District Police Station learned of the incident and ordered the local bailiff Yao Hongsheng to report it to the local court for verification. The deceased's son, Jia Rongquan, grieved over his father's tragic death, feeling that his own lack of effort in earning a living had caused his father's unrest in death. He submitted a tearful petition to the court, requesting that an autopsy be waived.

Female Customer Just Left, Three Robbers Suddenly Arrive; Undoubtedly a Gang 190

Xiangmao New Cloth Shop, located at the entrance of Lishe West Lane, Lishe Caichang opposite the South Railway Station on Lujiabang Road, was about to close at around eight o'clock the previous evening. Suddenly, two young women entered the shop to buy clothing material. The shop, naturally, attended to these customers as they came at night, and did not close the doors. The women chose silk fabrics worth over forty yuan. The shop clerk took the money to the counter. As the clerk was balancing the accounts, the women left. Suddenly, three robbers wearing long gowns broke in, pointed guns at the cashier, and ransacked the open cash register, taking over one hundred yuan in cash and a gold ring from a shop employee before fleeing. After the shop employees recovered from their shock, they reported the incident to the Lujiabang Police Station, which dispatched officers to the scene. However, the robbers had already vanished without a trace. The incident was reported to the Second District Headquarters for investigation. It is suspected that the women who made the purchase were part of the gang, acting as scouts to facilitate the robbery.

Hu Shanqing, the son of the late Hangzhou tycoon Hu Ganqing, and a shareholder in the Hu Qingyutang Pharmacy on Beijing Road and the Fuchang Ginseng Shop on Xian Gua Street in the Nanshi District, had a residence at No. 50 Guling Road. Resolution of the Incident Involving Forcibly Riding a Public Bus

Soldier Who Committed Assault Handed Over to Garrison Command 198

Second Station Chief of Seventh District Removed and Investigated

Third Platoon Leader Given Appropriate Punishment

A conflict occurred between a ticket seller and driver of a Chinese public bus in Zhabei and soldiers of the First Regiment of the Security Corps, resulting in multiple injuries. Details have been reported in this newspaper. The municipal government was extremely displeased with this unfortunate incident. Therefore, in addition to assuming responsibility for the injured parties' medical expenses, Mayor Wu decided to handle the matter with a strict and fair attitude, satisfying all parties and the company. He immediately ordered Xu Peihuang, director of the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau, Wen Hongen, director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and Zeng Zesheng, deputy director of the Security Corps, to dispatch personnel to jointly investigate and handle the matter, and set a deadline for reporting back. Director Wen, upon receiving the order, along with Chen Zhuomin, commander of the First Regiment of the Security Corps, visited the injured parties at the Yue Min Hospital on North Sichuan Road at 2:00 PM the day before yesterday to express their condolences. Li Dingzhong, the second station chief of the Seventh District, who witnessed the assault but failed to suppress it, was deemed to have disregarded his duties and was removed from his position for investigation. Special Article

The Crisis and Relief of China's Cotton Cloth Industry 205

— Zhang Rongchu

Cotton cloth is a necessity of life. Given the large population of the country and the expansion of consumption, it occupies an important position in national economics and international trade. Therefore, any drastic changes in national and world economics will inevitably affect China's cotton cloth industry. Domestic political changes and market prosperity and decline are directly affected. Even changes in the world economy and shifts in international relations will affect China's cotton cloth industry. During the European War, the cotton cloth industry temporarily broke free from the hegemony of imperialist economic forces and once flourished. Since the end of the European War, it has been subject to the long-term exploitation of imperialism every day. Up to the present, the situation of rural bankruptcy has been expanding, the resources of the national economy have been depleted, and ceaseless military and political turmoil, inland communication, and transportation have fallen into long-term obstruction. Under the attack of internal troubles and external invasions, the cotton cloth industry has fallen into extreme panic. Based on observations, the crises in China's cotton cloth industry are described below, hoping that compatriots across the country will be deeply aware.

(1) The Fall of the Northeast and the Sino-Japanese Shanghai War

Since the September 18th Incident, the Northeast market has been plundered by Japanese imperialists. The puppet organization, acting under the command of Japanese imperialism, erected strict tariff barriers, preventing cotton cloth from inland China from being sold to the three northeastern provinces. Consequently, cotton cloth factories that usually relied on the three northeastern provinces as their market saw sluggish sales, accumulated inventories, and fell into difficulty. They had no choice but to engage in suicidal competition, leading to a further decline in market prices. Since the outbreak of the Shanghai War, some Shanghai cotton cloth factories have been destroyed by artillery fire, while others have been affected by financial stagnation and cannot resume operations. Social economics have suffered huge losses of 140 million yuan, and the people's purchasing power has become even weaker. Therefore, the Northeast Incident and the January 28th Shanghai War have had a significant impact on China's industry, especially the cotton cloth industry.

(2) World Economic Panic and Dumping Policies

Since the tide of recession swept across the world, imperialist countries have been unable to remedy their own economic contradictions and have resorted to dumping policies as a last-ditch effort. China's cotton cloth industry has suffered even greater losses under the dumping policies of imperialism. Consumers only enjoy a few petty cheap benefits, while organic cotton cloth production organizations are broken up separately. In particular, Japanese imperialism has been deliberately plotting. After seizing our Northeast market, it is implementing active dumping in mainland China. Japanese merchants generally have abundant capital, low interest rates, complete equipment, superb technology, harmonious labor relations, and convenient transportation. The government also protects them. Therefore, in the past ten years, they have defeated Britain and the United States within China, aiming to monopolize the Chinese market, and wanting to keep all the people of China in a perpetual state of exploitation to satisfy their desires. (To be continued)

Letter to the Editor 206

To the Editor:

Regarding the news item published in your newspaper on the 21st of this month concerning the assault by soldiers of the security team and police officers of the Third Company of the Police Brigade on drivers and ticket sellers of the China Merchants Public Bus Company, resulting in a work slowdown, it is not consistent with the facts. On the afternoon of the 19th of this month, at 5:30 PM, four soldiers of the First Regiment of our Security Team, Ji Deshan, He Zhijun, Zeng Yuhuan, and Jiang Hongtai, had a misunderstanding with ticket sellers of a public bus in Section 5 of the 5th District, leading to a dispute. It was then immediately explained, and the matter was resolved. According to a letter from the company providing definitive proof, the incident of assaulting public bus drivers in Section 2 of the 7th District at 7:30 PM that afternoon, after investigation, was not committed by soldiers of this office. The China Merchants Bus Company has also provided a letter confirming that no soldiers from this office were involved, and the location and time were different from the previous incident. They were two completely separate matters, with no correlation whatsoever. The news item conflated the two, which is clearly inaccurate. Accordingly, a copy of the company's original letter is enclosed, requesting that your newspaper investigate and make the correction.

Sincerely,

Shanghai Security Office

Enclosed: One copy of the original letter

We are deeply grateful for your office's dispatch of Chief Wang Chengzhilin to our company to express condolences. The dispute between our company and the soldiers of your office in Section 5 of the 5th District in Jiangwan yesterday afternoon at 5:30 PM was a misunderstanding on both sides, and the matter was immediately explained. As for the assault on our company employees at Section 2 of the 7th District at approximately 7:00 PM, according to reports, no soldiers from your office were involved. The assailants were entirely members of the public, and it is a suspicious case. Our company intends to investigate the matter as the responsibility of the Public Security Bureau. Thank you for your inquiry. Respectfully submitted for your review.

Respectfully,

Shi Tifen [seal]

Reading Q&A

Reading "The Tale of Laughter and Tears" 209

(Continued)

Of course, this is not to say that "The Tale of Laughter and Tears" has already grasped the spirit of the times, or that "The Tale of Laughter and Tears" has fulfilled its profound social significance; on the contrary, "The Tale of Laughter and Tears" has not achieved this point. A great work with social significance, whether its depiction is on the affirmative side or the negative side, whether it exposes the sins of the declining class or inspires the growth of the emerging class, should exert its positivity as much as possible, and should set off the advancing social trend from that complex social life. However, what "The Tale of Laughter and Tears" grasps and describes are only some social bas-reliefs; passive, distorted, chaotic, and unintentional. Thus, in the structure of the whole story, it also forms a kind of "accidental" hodgepodge, unable to escape the trap of the legendary novel, "the performance is off track, unless the gods come to the rescue." Guan Xiugu in the style of "Thirteenth Sister" and Shou Feng who "exercises righteousness" appear only to complete those scenes of "weeding out the treacherous in the mountain temple" and "escaping the demon cave." Writing the Jianghu performers of Tianqiao into chivalrous figures like "divine dragons" who eliminate the strong and support the weak is already beyond reality, and attributing the fate of the evil warlords to the hand of a female knight "who exists in the sky but not in the world" is even more self-evident in its distortion of reality and escape from reality. "The Tale of Laughter and Tears," in terms of its social significance and in terms of its artistic evaluation, is a failure. It only superficially captures some fragmented social scenes, without selecting or refining them at all, and presenting the characteristics of that specific social life.

So, how does "The Tale of Laughter and Tears" catch its readers? As mentioned earlier, China's deformed society is reflected in people's lives and thoughts, also becoming deformed. Although what "The Tale of Laughter and Tears" captures are some bas-reliefs, this kind of fusion of different lifestyles of "ancient and modern" for thousands of years is precisely the place where it can cater to the tastes of the general floating urban class. The readers of "The Tale of Laughter and Tears" are undoubtedly those floating and unstable urban residents and the general bourgeoisie.

In a turbulent era, in the transition period from one society to another, the petty-bourgeois urban class is on the one hand pursuing the life of the bourgeois class who are addicted to pleasure, and on the other hand hating the evil society of the present. In "The Tale of Laughter and Tears," this kind of mass psychology just happens to project an stimulant.

The keynote of life depicted in "The Tale of Laughter and Tears" is full of the atmosphere of the enjoyment of life among bureaucrats and nobles. Not only is it not unusual for General Liu and others to spend a lot of money, but also the thirty or forty yuan for a pair of shoes for Mrs. Tao and the monthly thousand yuan for Miss He Lina to buy flowers can only make Fan Jiashu ashamed that he has "never seen the world." This extremely luxurious life is precisely the life that the general petty citizens pursue. However, what we should point out here is that the author completely ignores the negative aspects and only focuses on the affirmative description, only noticing its static posture, and not grasping its active direction. The luxurious life of aristocratic bureaucrats is only their own afterglow, another manifestation of their gradual collapse. The author does not develop the story in this way, but only evasively injects a kind of civilian thought into Fan Jiashu, causing him to avoid the noble and fashionable He Lina, and to love Shen Fengxi, who is involved in the dust; the result is that it emphasizes even more that He Lina also breaks away from her rich man, to the ultimate goal of "the gasoline lamplight in that room shines on a pair of figures, printed on the purple curtain." This method of expression just happens to cater to the psychology of those petty-citizen classes. In their journey to pursue the life of the bourgeois class, because of the limitations of social conditions, they encounter insurmountable obstacles, so they feel sad, so they feel disgusted, but they dare not seek a solution head-on. In helplessness, civilian thought inevitably becomes their self-consolation.

Like other martial arts love novels, "The Tale of Laughter and Tears" can also inject some temporary pleasure into the petty-bourgeois urban class. In China, the tyranny and cruelty of warlord bureaucrats, such as forcibly occupying Shen Fengxi, is the most common thing, and also the most infuriating thing. But most of China's petty bourgeoisie has a cowardly character. Characters like Ah Q fill this middle layer. They dare not face reality head-on, dare not raise their fists to fight in practice, so even if they are dissatisfied, even if they harbor resentment, they can only close themselves in the house and "swear at the sky and scold the earth" as a spiritual victory. This phenomenon, when expressed in politics, becomes the illusion of hoping for the appearance of a chivalrous person who eliminates the strong and helps the weak. In this book, Guan Shoufeng's loyalty and helping friends out of trouble, and Guan Xiugu's risking her life to "eliminate traitors for the people" can be said to be the scenes that make people feel the most happy. It is a pity that this kind of "weeding out traitors in the mountain temple" is neither something that exists in the present society, nor can it be used as a creed to enlighten the masses. This is just a drug made by writers who are influenced by the ruling class in feudal society to anesthetize the masses, and the author of "The Tale of Laughter and Tears" accepted this legacy without any reservations. On this point, the author of "The Tale of Laughter and Tears" cannot but say "it is truly regrettable."

In addition, "The Tale of Laughter and Tears" also embellishes some episodes of joys and sorrows, Fan Jiashu's initial "tender affection" with Shen Fengxi, and finally "splitting the volume and flying the moth," all of which are in line with the life interests of the bourgeois class.

The above can be said to have explained the reasons why "The Tale of Laughter and Tears" can be popular for a while. The author has completely seen through the floating psychology of the upper and middle social classes, and has fulfilled his responsibility in anesthetizing the masses and distorting reality. Because of this, we should further examine what the central idea it expresses is. (To be continued)

Referee Football Match 226

Zhonghua Defeats Western United 227

Western United Led 3 to 2 in the First Half

Overall Result: China United Wins 6 to 4

Members of the Shanghai Chinese and Western Referee Association held a football match at Shenyuan yesterday. Admission tickets were six corners each, and the proceeds were donated to the Catholic Youth Association for charity. There were only about 300 spectators. Many of the players in both teams were famous generals from the past, and their play was satisfactory. Western United was intimidating and led 3 to 2 in the first half. In the second half, they scored first again, making it 4 to 2. The Chinese team was in a precarious situation, but thanks to their final efforts, they reversed the defeat and won 6 to 4.

First Half 228

After the start of the match, the Western Union team launched a surprise attack, catching the Chinese team off guard. Pennell scored the first goal, barely two minutes after the kickoff. Two minutes later, Pennell scored again. The Chinese team, not to be outdone, launched a swift counterattack. With Lu Zhong'en's assistance, Dong Xiaopei shot from 20 yards out, and the Western Union goalkeeper fumbled the save. Later, from a corner kick, Pennell headed the ball in, and Lao Zhou lost control, putting Western Union ahead 3-2.

Second Half 229

During halftime, the veteran players had a hearty drink and continued the battle. After several rounds, neither side could score. Following a fifteen-minute stalemate, a Western Union player broke through and scored a goal, putting the Chinese team in a precarious 2-4 deficit. The players gave their all, launching a courageous counterattack. Dong Xiaopei succeeded instantly, and Qu Hongren charged straight ahead, leveling the score in a flash. Half an hour later, the portly Li Laoban (Baojun) also scored a goal. Lü Changfu scored the sixth goal in the last five minutes, allowing the Chinese team to escape from the brink of defeat and turn the tide.

Chinese Team

Zhou Jiaqi, Zhu Qiu, Shao Leping, Ni Xiaoben, Wu Shouchong, Lu Zhongen, Zhang Le, Qu Hongren, Chen Jixiang, Li Baojun, Dong Xiaopei, Chen Shunde, Lü Changfu. Western Union Team

Citywide First Workers' Games Ball Games Begin Today 234

Held at the Football Field and the Sports Field

Regulations and Staff List Announced Yesterday

The first citywide Workers' Games, sponsored by the Shanghai General Labor Union, is starting its ball games today, due to the large number of participants. The football and basketball championships will be held in advance at the China Football Field and the City No. 1 Sports Field, respectively. Before the games, the Union's photography team will be dispatched to take photos on site to prevent non-workers from participating in the competition, which would defeat the true meaning of the promotion and prevent abuses. If a team does not arrive within 15 minutes of the scheduled time, it will be considered a forfeit. Each football match will be 30 minutes, with teams switching sides. Each team will assign one linesman. Each basketball game will be 16 minutes, with teams switching sides. Each team should assign a record keeper. During the competition, both sides should absolutely obey the referee and should not stop the game without reason, and should uphold sportsmanship. It is now known that the opening ceremony will be held at 9:00 AM on May 5th, and the closing ceremony will be held at 6:00 PM on May 6th. In order to facilitate the participation of workers from all over the city, the event will still be held at the China Athletic Field as originally planned. The staff of the conference has been appointed, and it is said that the athletic staff of the conference is responsible for the competition group of the Union, and has sent letters to hire sports experts from this city, which will be announced soon. The regulations, staff list, and ball game schedule of the conference are listed below.

Conference Regulations 235

The regulations of the Shanghai General Labor Union Workers' Games are as follows: (Chapter 1) General Principles, Article 1: The name of this conference is the Shanghai General Labor Union Citywide Workers' Games. Article 2: The purpose of this conference is to promote public sports and improve workers' health. Article 3: This conference is held once every spring. Article 4: This conference is directly under the Executive Committee of the Shanghai General Labor Union. (Chapter 2) Organization, Article 5: This conference is composed of a sports committee consisting of five members appointed by the Shanghai General Labor Union, and several sports experts are hired (temporary decision) to organize it. Article 6: This conference has one preparatory director, and five sections: general affairs, publicity, documentation, communication, and guidance. Each section has a director and deputy director, all of whom are elected by the preparatory committee members. (Chapter 3) Participation, Article 7: The competition is based on labor unions and factories. However, if a worker does not have a labor union organization but wishes to participate in the competition individually, he may join after the factory provides proof and the conference approves it. Article 8: Each participating labor union and factory should appoint a responsible representative to lead the team. (Chapter 4) Championship, Article 9: The competition is divided into two types: championship and performance. Category A: Championship, temporarily set up the following five types: zi (field events), chou (track events), yin (soccer), mao (basketball), chen (tennis). Category B: Performance competition, temporarily divided into the following five types: zi (Chinese martial arts), chou (table tennis), yin (5000-meter race walk), mao (160-pound 100-meter weight race), chen (10,000-meter bicycle). Ji (additional performance can be added with the approval of this conference). Article 10: The unit with the most category championship wins will be the overall team championship winner. However, the scores of workers who do not have a labor union organization are not related to the overall team championship. If the team units obtain the same championship, the team with more track race scores will win the overall team championship. Article 11: This conference will provide prizes for outstanding teams or athletes as encouragement. Article 12: If a team or athlete violates any of the conference regulations, this conference may cancel their competition qualifications or other punishments. (Chapter 5) Expenses, Article 13: All expenses of this conference shall be listed in a list prepared by this conference and submitted to the City General Labor Union for allocation. (Chapter 6) Protest, Article 14: If any unit disagrees with the referee's decision, the responsible representative of the unit should submit a protest in writing within 24 hours after the game, and pay a protest fee of 5 yuan. However, if the conference considers the protest to be unreasonable, it will be confiscated. Article 16: The ruling of this conference is the highest ruling and no further protests may be lodged. (Chapter 7) Supplementary Provisions, Article 17: If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, this conference may amend them at any time. Article 18: These regulations shall be implemented after being approved by the committee and submitted to the City General Labor Union for approval.

Physical Education Instructors and Athletes Must Study Track and Field Techniques 236

Sports Experts Newly Compile Track and Field Books

The track and field season has arrived, and sports meets are being held everywhere. However, if athletes want to win and physical education teachers want to guide students, in addition to practicing more, they must read track and field books and study the latest methods in order to improve their skills. Otherwise, their efforts will be in vain and they will harm their bodies. The Diligent Bookstore at 554 Sima Road, Shanghai, has recently published many kinds of track and field books, all compiled by sports experts, such as "Track and Field Training Method" compiled by Zhang Heng (hardcover, two yuan), "Track and Field Referee Method" by Zhi Fuliang (six corners), "Five and Ten Item Training Method" compiled by Ruan Weicun and proofread by Hao Gengsheng (nine corners and a half), "Before the Female Athlete Arrives at the City" written by World Female Track and Field Star Hitomi Kinu (nine corners), "Elementary School Track and Field" compiled by Ruan Weicun and proofread by Sun Hebin (three corners), and "Liu Changchun's Success Story in Sprinting" compiled by Jiang Huaiqing and proofread by Song Junfu (three corners). In addition to instructing on the theory and latest techniques of track and field, the above books also have pictures to illustrate athletic postures. Reading them is like having a good teacher. There are also "Middle School Sports Meet Guide" written by Wang Fuliang (six corners) and "Elementary School Sports Meet Guide" written by Xiang Xianggao (six corners and a half), which detail the procedures for organizing sports meets, competition methods, evaluation standards, applied equipment, etc. Anyone organizing a sports meet who buys and reads a copy can proceed smoothly and achieve good results. In order to give preferential treatment to comrades in the sports field, the Bureau is offering a 10% discount on all books, with postage added as required.

Other Provinces: Zhejiang Guidance Conference Closes 242

Closing Ceremony Held in the Morning, Aviation School Visited in the Afternoon

The 5th Zhejiang Provincial Local Education Guidance Conference was held yesterday (21st) for the third day. More than 70 representatives from various counties attended. At 8:00 AM, the Education Department invited Ma Xunbo, President of Zhejiang Provincial Japanese Remedial School, to give a lecture on autonomy and education. The main points were: 1. Education should aim at local autonomy; 2. Local autonomy should be achieved through education. He also reported on the educational facilities in Jiangning Experimental County, Jiangsu. At 9:30 AM, the closing ceremony was held. Qian Jiaqi, Secretary of the Education Department, presided over the ceremony. After the etiquette was completed, the Chairman gave a closing speech, stating that the 5th Guidance Conference has come to a successful conclusion, which is very gratifying. However, at this time of serious national crisis, all of us in the education field should shoulder the responsibility of reviving the dead hearts and striving to cultivate talents for the country, so that China can find a way out. Then, the heads of various departments reported on the visit to the Aviation School this afternoon, and in the evening, the Museum and the Department will screen a movie about the situation in the Northwest. The situation of the second and third conferences of the conference is recorded below.

Second Conference 243

Attendees: Hu Chengshu, Lin Ben He Naixian, He Yulong, Lu Lu Qimei, Jin Haiguan, Fei Shu, Hu Feng, Wang Ning Shi, Xu Xudong, Wang Xianyuan and other 63 people, chaired by Luo Dixian, recorded by Hu Baoliang and Ling Dujian, items for discussion,

1. Request the Department of Education to hold a training program for county school district guidance personnel. Resolved: The original draft in the examination report was rejected. 2. Counselors of central primary schools should attend the county guidance conference. Resolved: In the title, reason, and method, add one city character below the county character. The rest is passed according to the examination report. 3. The county guidance conferences are often held simultaneously in three or four counties, and the affiliated school counselors cannot attend and guide them one by one. Please find a way to remedy this. Resolved: According to the examination report, the revisions are as follows: (1) The title is proposed to be changed to "The dates of the county and city guidance conferences shall be arranged by the county and city education bureaus or sections before the start of the school year so that the guidance agencies can send personnel to attend and provide guidance." (2) Add the word "city" below the word "county" in the reasons and methods. (3) Reason 1: Change "Inform the attached school" to "Inform the guidance agency", change "Although the attached school clearly knows the conflict" to "Although the guidance agency clearly knows the conflict", and change "Various guidance agencies" to "Various guided agencies". (4) Reason 2: Change the four words "Teachers of attached schools" to "Staff of guidance agencies". (5) Reason 3: "Because the representatives of the attached schools did not attend" was changed to "Because the guidance agencies did not send personnel to attend". (6) Cancel Method 2 and change it to "The dates of the county and city guidance conferences shall be arranged by the county and city education bureaus or sections before each academic year, and submitted to the provincial school district guidance conference for review and approval." 4. Request the provincial government to issue an order to the local transportation agencies that all education guidance personnel in this province should be allowed to ride for free when traveling on official business to save public funds and facilitate guidance. 5. Request the Department of Education to find a way to provide half-price travel expenses for guidance personnel working outside. Resolved: The above two cases were discussed together and rejected according to the examination report. 6. Organize a production education research committee. Resolved: It was revised and approved according to the examination report: (1) The title was changed to "Proposed request to the Department of Education to organize a production education research association." (2) The method was changed to "Submit a request to the Department of Education to organize a production education research association to guide the implementation of production education in various counties and cities." 7. Submit a request to the Department of Education to order all county and city social education agencies to consistently contact local people from all walks of life to effectively promote the New Life Movement to revive the nation. Resolved: Except for deleting the two words "social" in the title, the rest was passed according to the examination report. 8. Submit a request to the Department of Education to order all counties and cities to complete the county school district social education guidance leading agencies as soon as possible. Resolved: It was passed according to the examination report. From 1:30 PM, Chen Da Xie and Li Yide were invited to give lectures. The conference continued from 4:00 PM. In the evening, the Department of Education hosted a banquet for all representatives at Jufeng Garden.

Third Conference 244

The third conference was held at 4:00 PM on the 20th, chaired by Qian Jiazhi, and recorded by Ling Dujian and Hu Baoliang. Items for discussion: 1. 23rd Annual Provincial Middle School Affiliated Primary School Guidance Standards for Elementary Education in Various Counties and Cities. Resolved: Except that "Provincial Middle School" was changed to "Provincial School" in the title and in each article, the rest was passed according to the examination report. 2. The county education bureaus should increase the guidance fee for central primary schools to improve guidance efficiency. Resolved: It was passed according to the examination report. 3. Resolved: It was passed according to the examination report. 5. The provincial school district social education guidance agencies should contact social education agencies in the district to hold joint activities. Resolved: It was passed according to the examination report. 6. Organize a provincial school district itinerant lecture group. Resolved: It was passed according to the examination report. 7. The provincial or provincial school district substitute social education guidance agencies should hold summer training classes for teachers of people's schools. Resolved: Except for adding the nine words "Contact the education bureaus and sections of various counties and cities" above the two words "Hold" in the title, the rest was passed according to the examination report. 8. The provincial or provincial school district social education guidance agencies and the education bureaus of various counties should strive to contact each other to increase the efficiency of guidance work. Resolved: According to the review opinion, this case need not be established. 9. Promote education for rural people to save the rural decline. Resolved: It was revised and approved according to the review opinion. 10. The schools specially established in various industrial areas should be affiliated with the same practical research institute of folk education. Resolved: It was passed according to the examination report. 12. Submit a request to the Department of Education that the provincial guidance subsidy fees for the provincial school district social education guidance agencies should be transferred to the Ministry of Finance by monthly letter from the next year, and should be allocated by the local business tax bureaus to facilitate business. Resolved: It was passed according to the examination report. 13. All counties and cities in this province should improve the folk inherent tunes, storytelling blind words as a tool for the implementation of folk education. Resolved: It was revised and approved according to the examination report. 14. It is suggested that the Department of Education organize a social education communication research department and a social education lecture class to facilitate the advancement of social education colleagues. Resolved: It was passed according to the examination report.

Ministry of Education Explains the Level of Nursing School Students 245

The Ministry of Education issued an order to the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau to explain matters related to nursing schools, instructing four points: (1) The two words "nursing" in the Senior Nursing Vocational School may be used interchangeably with the two words "nurse". (2) Senior nursing or nurse vocational schools shall not run junior level schools. Those who enroll students with elementary school graduation should be set to graduate in five years. (3) They should be handled in accordance with the procedure for private schools. (referring to the filing procedures) (4) The length of schooling for senior nurse vocational schools is set to three years. Those who enroll students with elementary school graduation are set to five years. The courses taught can be implemented with reference to the regulations on the teaching subjects and class hours of each department of the vocational schools promulgated by the Ministry. The detailed teaching syllabus is being compiled by the Ministry.

Recently, it was learned that the president of the school, Chen Yuguang, has obtained the permission of Finance Minister Kong and decided to issue 100,000 from the face value of the 22-year customs treasury bills, which will be transferred by the Central Bank.

Local

Various Academic Groups: Continued Records of Hainan Biological Collection 248

Divided into Land and Sea Teams to Engage in Collection

The Second Batch of Personnel Will Depart from Beijing

The Hainan Biological Collection Group, organized by the Chinese Science Society and other six academic groups, has safely arrived in Hainan Island after joining the staff of the Guangdong and Guangxi Geological Survey Institute. It has been reported before. Now it is learned that the group is divided into land and sea teams to carry out their work for the convenience of collection.

On the Land Team Side 249

Led by Liu Xian, it is divided into three groups: anthropology, geology, and zoology. The leaders of the Li people are responsible for leading the work along the way. They have reached Shengyan from Wuzhi Mountain and met with the animal group. Shengyan is surrounded by mountains on all sides, 1,100 feet above sea level. The collection group set up the land team's headquarters here. The transportation here is convenient and the food is abundant, which is suitable for the collection and rest of terrestrial animals. However, it is still early, so all kinds of animals are very few. Only the specimens of reptiles and amphibians are relatively more.

Naval Forces 250

Led by Wang Yikang, they are currently at the estuary. Huangsha Hanhan [deserted land] has very few livestock and animals. The biological collectors have nothing to be attached to. The east of the estuary is also a beach, and the coastline is especially barren and has nothing to hunt. Only the Sanya port in the south has abundant marine resources, making collection easier. After completing work at the estuary, they plan to go to Lingshui, where there are more reefs, and the harvest should be better than in the north of Yazhou. Currently, in addition to fish and shrimp, they are also collecting parasites, but the amounts are very small. It is estimated that they will reach Beili by mid-May, and then return to the estuary along the northwest coast. Within half a year, they can tour Qiongzhou Island. The second group of collectors will also depart from Nanjing for work at the end of this month.

The Shanghai Boy Scout Friendship Competition was held yesterday at the Nanyang Group Drill Ground, details of which have been reported in this newspaper. The news of the first day of the competition is reported below:

Those present from the group affairs included Zheng Run Sang, Director of the Preparatory Committee for the Boy Scout Friendship Competition; Xu Zicheng, Director of the Campground; Cao Yunxiang, Director of General Affairs; Ma Xie Ai Wu Shutang, Director of Interviewing; Yu Kuaiyuan, Cai Haomin, and Wu Xusheng, members of the Preparatory Committee; Shen Shukui, Shen Tongyi, Shen Baochang, Wang Gang, Zhao Bangheng, Guan Jun, Sun Enlin, and Yu Yuanjue, judges, and more than twenty others. Visitors included Xi Youchang, leader of the Chengai Troupe, who led the scouts into the arena.

Inspection Ceremony: At about 2 PM, Zheng Runsang, Director of the Preparatory Committee for the Friendship Competition, and others gathered the Boy Scouts from various teams, who entered the arena in an orderly fashion and stood on the side of the road to hold a flag-raising ceremony. Subsequently, judges Shen Shukui, Shen Tongyi, and Wang Gang delivered speeches one after another, all of which were extremely sincere and moving.

Drill Competition: At about 3 PM, each team held a drill competition. Each team consisted of ten people, and the time limit was ten minutes. The Boy Scouts of each team were extremely agile in their movements, and their formations were solemn and majestic. It can truly be said that each was uniquely brilliant. In the evening, there were also entertainment performances, and the enthusiasm was still strong.

A Glimpse of the Campground: West of the headquarters was the Nanyang Group's base camp, including (1) Black Eagle, (2) Leopard Team, (3) Lion Team, (4) Horse Team, a total of four teams. To the northwest were the John Group's Flying Eagle Team, Hound Team, Guangyi Group's Tiger Team, Leopard Team, Yucai Group's Eagle Team, Guangdong Group's Wolf Team, Ningbo Group's Second Primary School's Horse Team and Deer Team, Ningbo First Primary School's Lion Team, and the Youth Moral Education Association's Eagle Team, a total of seven groups and fifteen small teams. Looking at the arrangement of each camp, the Nanyang Group's was the most eye-catching. Each camp had a gate erected, with the name and zodiac sign of each team added to it, decorating the space. Visitors passing through the gate would know the name of the camp. The arrangements of the other teams were also quite neat and excellent.

Today's Competition: Today is the last day of the competition. There will be morning exercises at 6:30 AM, breakfast at 7:30 AM, knot-tying competition at 9:00 AM, lunch at 12:00 PM, regulations competition starting at 1:00 PM, camp packing at 4:00 PM, and the closing of the camping at 5:00 PM. According to the reporter, the "Boy Scout Group Regular Joint Camping" mentioned in yesterday's newspaper refers to the Friendship Competition held by Nanyang, John, and other schools.

Municipal Zoo Actively Preparing for Milk Cow Competition 253

The Shanghai Municipal Zoo, in order to promote public production and improve the breed of milk cows, has obtained approval from the Municipal Board of Education to hold the first Milk Cow Competition. The event is scheduled for May 27th, and registration has already begun yesterday. All Chinese citizens who raise milk cows are welcome to participate, with a limit of one head per breed. Excellent bulls may also participate in the exhibition. Breeds are temporarily divided into Dutch, Jianshan, and Gengci. All participants must send their competing milk cows along with their registration certificates to the meeting place before 1 PM on May 27th. The meeting place has been decided to be the vacant lot of the Penglai Market on Penglai Road. Those wishing to arrange various promotional materials in the venue must first report to the zoo for permission, at their own expense. The selection of judges and various prizes is currently underway.

Special Feature

The Current Situation of Secondary Education in England 257

(Continued)

— Zhu Zhensun

(VIII) Coeducation

In England, coeducation is rarely seen, except in some primary schools in London. However, in other places, coeducation is very common. In the whole of England, the number of coeducational schools exceeds the number of single-sex schools. This coeducation is partly to save money, but partly based on educational principles. In fact, many British educators believe that coeducation is a special stage in education.

(IX) Teacher Salaries

There are about two different standards for the salaries of secondary school teachers in England, namely those with degrees and those without degrees. For teachers with degrees, the salary ranges from £276 to £528 for men, with an annual increase of £15, up to eighteen years. For women, the salary ranges from £264 to £420, with an annual increase of £14, up to fourteen years. For teachers without degrees, the salary ranges from £204 to £432 for men, with an annual increase of £15, up to twenty years. For women, the salary ranges from £192 to £342, with an annual increase of £9, up to eighteen years. All secondary school teachers who retire between the ages of sixty and sixty-five can receive half of their total service period as a pension.

(X) Central Schools

There are about one hundred central schools in London, England. This kind of school is not a complete middle school, because it only has a four-year program, which is quite similar to our junior high school. In the first two academic years, students must study the same subjects, including modern foreign languages. In the last two academic years, students learn more knowledge in the fields of commerce or industry. The purpose of this school is to provide students with preparation for employment. The curriculum of Stanley Central School (which is more focused on industry) is described below for reference:

(1) Bible, (2) English, (3) German, (4) Geography, (5) History, (6) Mathematics, (7) Chemistry, (8) Physics, (9) Drawing and Art, (10) Carpentry and Metalworking, (11) Music, (12) Gymnastics.

Central schools are tuition-free, so many people want to enter. However, because the number of places is limited, competition is fierce. It selects students based on the results of the primary school scholarship examination that students should take at the age of eleven. Students who have not obtained a place in a middle school may be able to obtain a good position in a central school, because they still have the opportunity to participate in the central school examination at the age of thirteen. Students who have not obtained a place in either middle school or central school must enter a senior primary school for remedial studies until the age of fourteen. The work in this school is mostly manual activity.

Central schools can be called middle schools in terms of appearance and spirit, because the students inside are treated as adult male and female students. All the male and female teachers are also experts, and their level is the same as that of the male and female teachers in the middle schools, but their salaries are lower.

The Spirit of Martialism 258

— Guo Pinjuan

Little friends: Do you know why we Chinese are called "sick men of East Asia" by foreigners? What a shameful title this is!

In the past, we Chinese valued scholars too much and despised martial artists. Therefore, not only did students who studied want to be refined people, but other people also envied being refined people. As a result, they did not pay attention to exercise or physical education, and did not exercise their bodies, making everyone weak and sickly.

Little friends: Think about it, a person with a body as weak as a sick man, even if he is very knowledgeable, what can he do for the country? No wonder our China is getting weaker and weaker, and no wonder foreigners ridicule us as "sick men of East Asia"! In this world of the survival of the fittest, weak nations will be eliminated, and only by having the spirit of martialism can they survive. Little friends: Do you want to wash away the shame of the "sick men of East Asia"? Do you want to create great undertakings? Do you want China to become strong? Then everyone must have the spirit of martialism!

Stone Child 259

— Yuan Xifu

Little friends, do you want to hear the story of the Stone Child? I will tell you the story now. Poor Jiading! During the Ming Dynasty, it was often disturbed by Japanese pirates who robbed things, burned houses, and killed people. The magistrate at that time, Yin Fenglin, was a confused old man who didn't know anything. The people outside the city had no choice but to escape into the city. The detestable Japanese pirates wanted to attack the city again. Fortunately, there were soldiers and common people on the city walls, guarding it day and night, so they were not able to break through.

One night, the people guarding the city were all too tired to sleep, and the Japanese pirates climbed up the city walls again. The people guarding the city didn't know it yet, when suddenly a child shouted loudly, "The bandits are coming! The bandits are coming!" The people guarding the city heard it and quickly got up to kill the bandits, killing quite a few of them.

After the bandits left, everyone went to look for the child who had shouted, but who knew that the poor child had already been killed by the bandits!

Later, people commemorated him by carving a stone statue of the child and erecting it on the northwest gate of Jiading City, where it is still preserved today!

Why Do Birds Fight? 260

— Xu Zongjie

Darwin once said, "The fighting of birds occurs because the males are fighting for females, which can be said to be for love." After research by many zoologists, it was only known that this statement was not very reliable. Because when they fight, the males and males, and the females and females, all join the battle, pairing off to fight. From this point of view, they are definitely not fighting for love.

Originally, according to Howard, the fighting of birds is for territory, which can also be said to be for food. Because after they find a suitable branch and make a nest, they will no longer allow other birds to stay here. And the area around this nest seems to be under its jurisdiction, and other birds are not allowed to forage for food. If a bird invades its sovereignty, it will definitely rise up and fight. Little friends, even birds know how to protect their territory, what should we humans do?

Tomb Sweeping 261

— Bo Zhen

On a bright spring day, we left our hometown to sweep the tombs of our ancestors in the countryside.

We sat silently on a sturdy steamboat. At that time, the boat was very crowded, and I was squeezed inside, almost unable to breathe. There were men and women, old and young. Some were talking and laughing, some were eating, and some were leaning out the window to look at the scenery.

I also looked out the window and saw fields full of golden rape flowers, and rows of weeping willows swaying in the breeze on both sides of the bank.

We arrived at our destination. It was almost noon.

After passing through a dense forest, crossing several shallow swamps, and walking along uneven mountain roads, we arrived at our tomb.

A pile of yellow earth, this is the resting place of our ancestors. There was also a stone table placed in front of it, and we arranged the sacrificial dishes on the table. We lit incense and candles and burned paper money, kowtowing one by one.

At the same time, my grandmother kept saying, "May the ancestors bless our whole family with health and peace!"

Alas! Buried in this pile of yellow earth are several decaying coffins. The bodies of the ancestors have long since become skeletons. Life is gone too. Was what my grandmother said addressed to those skeletons? This is really a superstitious act of the old ladies.

Little friends, do you also have grandmothers? It's probably the same, right.
