Can Eyes Be Wrong? 264

— Jiang Yan

Little friends, you can look at the picture before reading the text.

After looking at the picture, don't you feel that the lines in each picture are of different lengths? But, you are wrong. If you don't believe it, you can take a ruler to measure them. Let me tell you, they are all the same length.

After measuring them, do you have some thoughts? -- Why are eyes wrong?

Let me tell you, our eyes are unreliable. They often give us errors, and some are even unable to see. Therefore, next time you do anything, you should not just look with your eyes. It is necessary to use your brain to examine and consider.

Economic Iron 265

— Zhaode

Little friends, aren't your school uniforms often washed? Do you hire someone to wash them? Or does your mother wash them for you? How are they after drying? Aren't they very wrinkled and unpresentable? Apart from using an iron, have you ever thought of an economic iron to iron them flat? If you haven't thought about it, now I will tell you about an economic iron that I have used before! The so-called economic iron does not need charcoal! Then you must ask, if you don't use charcoal, what do you use? What is its shape? What is it made of? Please don't panic! It is an enamelware that every family has! A tooth powder can (but it should be a little bigger). If you pour boiling water into it and close the lid, then the economic iron is successful! You can use it to iron clothes and trousers. It is not only light and convenient, but also economic, and ironing clothes is no different from a real iron!

Little friends, you might as well try it with your dried and wrinkled clothes!

Orphan 266

— Shi Yusheng

His face was pale yellow, with two small, crimson lips, showing an undernourished look. But those black, shiny eyes could no longer hide his lively soul, gently, gently turning, like a pair of little lambs, endearing.

"Yuan"! Once I asked him: "Why are you so thin?"

"Sir! I don't eat often!" He lowered his head.

"Oh! What do you eat?"

"Four copper coins, two yuanzi [glutinous rice balls]!" He trembled.

"Don't you like to eat rice?"

"No, rice is late, I'm afraid I won't make it to class!" He raised his head.

"Doesn't your mother feel sorry for you?"

"My mother left me when I was two years old!" His eyes turned red, "I followed my aunt,..."

"What about your father?" I held him tightly.

"Oh, sir! Not long ago, one night, I became an or...orphan again!" He cried.

Small Experience 267

— Jianfen

Wiping Slate Little friends: Does your school use slates for copying books? Do you copy the words from the books onto the slate with a slate pencil? After the slate is full of words, don't you have to wipe them off? If you use a dry piece of paper or a dry cloth to wipe it, then the slate pencil powder written on the slate will fly up; if you accidentally breathe it in, it will be harmful to your lungs. But what can you do? Just before you wipe the slate pencil marks off the slate, first pour some water on the slate, and then wipe it with paper or cloth; or directly use a wet piece of paper or a wet cloth to wipe it, it is the same. This way, the slate pencil powder will not fly up. Inkstone Little friends: If your inkstone has been used for a long time, won't there be a lot of accumulated ink around the inkstone? At this time, do you feel that it is very difficult to grind ink? And if you are not careful, when grinding ink, if the ink touches the accumulated ink on the inkstone, the ink will splash out, even splashing on your clothes. Isn't this very annoying? If you encounter this situation, I hope you quickly wash off the accumulated ink on the inkstone; then not only will it be easy to grind thick ink, but it will also save effort. P.S. If the teacher asks you to wipe the words written on the blackboard with chalk; you can do it according to the "Wiping Slate" method, then the chalk dust will not fly into your nose and mouth. Your inkstone, even if it does not have accumulated ink around it, can also be washed once every Sunday; although your hands will suffer a little, it is much better to grind ink with it than with an inkstone that has not been washed.

Honesty and Lying 268

— Jin Yong

Little friends! Don't you like to hear stories very much? Now I will tell you one.

Once upon a time, there was a woodcutter chopping trees by the river. By chance, his axe fell into the river and sank. The woodcutter lost his beloved axe and was very sad. The river god heard him. He took a golden axe from the river and gave it to him. The woodcutter did not admit that it was his original axe. The river god dived into the river again and took out a silver axe, but he still did not admit it. Finally, the river god took out the axe he had lost and gave it to him. So, he happily thanked the river god for his virtue. The river god loved him very much for being honest, so he gave him the golden axe and the silver axe as well.

Later, this news was known to one of his friends. He also wanted to get rich. So, he disguised himself as a woodcutter and chopped trees by the river; deliberately throwing his axe into the river. So, he sat by the river and cried loudly. The river god heard his crying and ran to ask him why he was crying? He pretended to say, "Because I lost my axe." The river god still dived into the river and took out a golden axe.

"Yes, that's really my axe!" He couldn't help saying in his heart:

The river god was furious. He scolded him fiercely for not telling the truth, and he didn't even give him the axe he had dropped!

Little friends! You should be honest children. In the story above, it is very clear that honesty is very beneficial to your life.

Letters from Little Friends in the Countryside 269

— Ziming

Big Classroom

Dear Little Friends:

Where do you read? You probably all read in classrooms with doors and windows. You want to gain knowledge, and you only seek it in a stereotyped way in books. But, let me test you: I will take two stalks of wheat, one is barley, and one is wheat. Answer honestly, can you tell them apart? We often encounter plant researchers coming to the countryside, but they still can't recognize many plant names!

Our classroom doesn't have doors, the forest is our research place, the river beach is our place for leisure activities, and those fields and mounds are where we read. Our books are a leaf, a beautiful flower. Those planted in the fields, swimming in the rivers, flying in the sky, growing on the ground, all of these are our living books; because they are living, they arouse a lot of learning interest in us. We call this kind of learning place the "Big Classroom"; except for the rare times when we read dull books in the classroom indoors, most of the time is spent in the Big Classroom.

The air in the Big Classroom is fresh, our bodies are comfortable, and our spirits are refreshed; the content of the books is rich, whatever we want to study, we have it; astronomy, geography, there are living things, and there is non-living things, we have everything; no wonder all the great scientists since ancient times have graduated from the "Big Classroom".

Sleeping Postures of Animals 270

— Wang Hengjiu

Dear Little Friends! Previously, Mr. Fan told us about the sleeping postures of several animals in "The Sleep of Animals." This is indeed very meaningful. Here, I will just add a little bit of information.

Short-legged and fat beasts, such as elephants, rhinoceroses, hippos, etc., when they sleep, they first bend their legs and put them under their stomachs, and then lie down, stretching their four legs straight. Carnivorous beasts such as lions, tigers, and leopards sleep like cats. There is also a giraffe, also known as a unicorn, which always bends its head over and places it on its lower back when sleeping. When bears sleep, they always hide their heads in their bodies; however, there is a peculiar bear in America that is very lazy. When sleeping, it hangs its four feet upside down on tree branches, like a bat, grasping the branches with its claws. When we look at it, we feel that this sleeping method is very laborious, but in fact, its feet are very strong. The more soundly it sleeps, the tighter its feet grasp the branches. Little friends, do you think it's strange?

Also, domestic rabbits and squirrels simply don't look like they are sleeping when they sleep, they just shrink into a ball. Others, such as birds, chickens, and herons among the birds, always stand upright and still when sleeping, hiding their heads under their own wings.

Dear Little Friends! The above are all strange sleeping methods of animals, but there are many others! Due to space limitations, I can't write any more.

New Life 271

— Mr. Ma Peiyuan's Speech, Recorded by Zhang Rui

Today, I'm here to talk to you, children, about new life. First, we need to understand what we mean by "life." Life is the activity of human beings seeking survival. Whether it's agriculture, industry, commerce, academics, or politics... it's all life. So, what is called "new life"? New life is a meaningful life. And what is a meaningful life? Now, let me give you an example to illustrate: For instance, yesterday, Uncle Wang didn't go to work in the fields but instead went to the street to gamble, losing all but twenty-three yuan of his hundred-yuan money for selling the ox. He was upset and went to a tavern, ate three catties of sorghum, drank a bottle of old wine, and drunkenly ran home, fighting with his wife. The next morning, he woke up and felt he shouldn't have gambled yesterday. He shouldn't have drunk and certainly shouldn't have fought with his wife. Thinking this, he immediately went to the kitchen and apologized to his wife. His wife asked him, "Since you knew you were doing wrong yesterday, why did you do such a wrong thing?" Uncle Wang was speechless, and could only smile and walk away. Children! Do you think Uncle Wang's life has meaning? So I say, whatever you do, be able to first ask "Why?"—Why this way? Why not that way? Being able to answer this "why" is a meaningful life, which is what we call new life. The scope of new life is very broad, whether it's political, economic, social, or educational. So I hope you children will also live a meaningful new life in the future! As for what your new life as children should be like, please think about it carefully!

Finance: US President Opposes Silver Legislation; Bullion Recovers by $1.70 273

Fluctuations Narrow, Transaction Volume Average

Yesterday, the gold market saw the future of silver remain uncertain, resulting in a rebound. The situation in the first half of the day was weak but resilient, and market sentiment was good. In the morning, overseas silver markets rose in both the UK and the US. The forward silver price on the Five Metals Exchange also rose by 0.5 to 1.5%. Exchange rates trended upwards. London spot gold fell by half a penny. US cotton rose by 3 points, US wheat by 8.75. Stocks rose by $1.03. The opening price for wool was withdrawn to $62.30. According to an Associated Press report, the US President was still unlikely to agree to silver measures. Dadecheng, Zhaofengchang, and others entered the market, pushing the price up to $6. Foreign dispatches also contained rumors of increased gold prices. Fuxing, Yongheng, and others sold, pushing the price back to $4.50. Later, a Reuters dispatch reported that the President and silver faction leaders began a meeting on Saturday evening. The White House stated that the President did not want any silver legislation to pass in the current Congress and that he believed he was in a good position to resist any mandatory silver legislation within the current Congress. The White House further stated that the President felt it would be impossible to address silver issues without cooperating with countries around the world. The situation then stabilized, and the price of silver fell slightly in the Seattle night market, causing the gold price to rise. Although there was a slight dip at one point in the morning, major players continued to enter the market, and the market continued to stabilize at the close. The trading range was limited in the first half of the day, and transactions were average. The price of red gold was $981. Swaps continued to be weak. The market situation for the first half of the day is recorded below.

The market opened at $964.90, slightly down by 30 cents from the previous close. Goods opened at the same price. The exchange market opened with the near-term selling price for British exchange at 1 shilling 4 pence 0625, and for US exchange at $34.625. Hengyuanyuan, Kangxiang, Yida, and Yong bought, pushing the price up to $6.50. HSBC listed British exchange at half a shilling and US exchange at 12.5 cents. Hengxing, Hengyu, Tianfeng, Zhifeng, Yongying, and Fengheng sold, pushing the price back to $5. Duyi bought September US dollars at 12.5 cents. Zhengjin took August at $35. Hengxing, Hengchang, and Yongjin were stable, but because Zhejiang plugged July US dollars at 8.75 cents, spot supply was available, struggling around $6. However, the domestic market was tight. Mitsui bought August US dollars at $35 and September at 12.5 cents. Zhifeng, Yongfu, Xingyong, Dasheng, Hengyu, Yida, Yongheng, Hengxing, and others entered the market, reaching $7. Goods were slightly weaker due to supply, but Hengxing and Yida Yong continued to enter the market due to the night market silver price falling by half a cent, pushing the price to $7.20. Yuqing Yong and Yida Yong sold, retreating, and Jiatai, Hengyu, Dadecheng, Qianchang, and Xiang also sold, dropping to $6. Hengxing entered again and recovered, then fell to $5.60. Fuchang and Qingfayong bought at low prices, and Dekang raised prices. The market gradually rose to $966.90 at noon. Goods were traded at $7.10. Fuchang continued to enter the market after the close, making it more stable. The highest price in the first half of the day was $967.20, and the lowest was $964.90, fluctuating by $2.30. As a result, the market rose by $1.70 compared to the previous close.

Settlement prices reflected HSBC's US exchange listing rising by 12.5 cents to $34.125, resulting in a standard gold price of $1014. Based on the closing price, approximately $47 was squeezed, down $5 from the previous close. The registered price for May was $975, and for June was $967. The morning water supplement was $975. The price of red gold was $981. The spot red gold market was average. The Tianjin group sold over 2,500 taels to Yingfenghang, Dadecheng, Tongfenghang, and Dafengheng at an additional $16.50. Over 4,000 taels of Eastern goods arrived, or were delivered at an additional price of $15.25 and $15. In addition, secondary goods with a purity of 985 were sold by Taikangrun to the customer group for over 400 taels at an additional $10.05. The swap market opened at around $5. Dadecheng and Yingfenghang immediately came in to make up the difference. The Dalian group successfully swapped out quite a bit, but all the spot traders were willing to swap out, gradually falling from $4.90. Grain: Futures Flour Continues to Find New Low Prices 282

Yesterday's flour market, after opening in the morning, prices for each month initially showed stability. With the quotation of foreign wheat in Chicago slightly better by around 0.2 yuan and in Canada significantly better by around 0.08 yuan, the market sentiment after opening was slightly stable. Opening prices for each month were slightly better by 0.005 yuan compared to the previous day. However, the buying interest from both inside and outside the industry was truly impossible to stimulate. As far as merchant groups were concerned, only spot transactions were of interest; the focus on forward transactions was not as strong as before because general commodity prices were still generally declining. Therefore, prices fell again in subsequent trading sessions. By the afternoon opening, prices for each month stepped into decline again, and new record low prices for each month gradually emerged. The current month initially opened at 0.02 yuan, but later decreased to 2.0005 yuan, showing a trend of approaching the 2 yuan level. May also broke through to below 2 yuan. All other months saw a consistent and sharp decline. This situation is actually due to weak purchasing power, and those within and outside the industry do not dare to harbor thoughts of speculation, so the situation is getting worse and worse, making it even more unthinkable. As a result, prices fell again by 0.02 yuan, May fell by 0.0225 yuan, June fell by 0.015 yuan, July fell by 0.0175 yuan, August fell by 0.02 yuan, and September fell by 0.0075 yuan.

Futures Wheat: Market Continues to Decline 283

Yesterday's futures wheat market, after opening in the morning, prices for each month generally showed stability. With the quotation of foreign wheat recovering by around 0.2 or 0.08 yuan, the market sentiment at the time of opening turned slightly stable, and the selling pressure from within the industry also paused slightly. Prices for each month were similar to the previous fluctuations. By the afternoon opening, the situation quickly and gradually deteriorated. Initially due to the clear weather, and later due to the falling prices of futures flour, the market became nervous, and prices loosened again. The fundamental reason is that after the devastation of the rural areas, there are very few opportunities for commodity prices to rise. The current month, due to the poor flour market and the abundant arrival of spot wheat, saw a significant drop in opening prices. The far-term, with June being the weakest, fell as low as 3.30 yuan. As a result, the current month fell by 0.06 yuan, June fell by 0.03 yuan, and August fell by 0.01 yuan. Spot wheat, due to the significant decline in standards and the closure of mills, saw no trading.

Silk and Tea: Consolidated Report on Sericulture in Jiangsu and Zhejiang 286

(Delayed Development of Silkworm Eggs in Zhejiang) "Gaoshi" ordered farmers this year to breed improved varieties. During the hatching period, the weather was unusually cold, and the silkworms hatched unevenly. The early batches had already completed two molts and were feeding on leaves for three or four days. The late batches were only just beginning to feed on leaves after the first molt. "Sanbao": The number of farmers raising silkworms this year is less than two-thirds of last year. The number of eggs hatched is also small. In addition, the silkworms hatched at different times, with a difference of about a week. The early silkworms will have completed two molts and have sufficient leaves. The late silkworms are only feeding on leaves for three or four days. Guidance officers are assisting with tasks such as stimulating hatching and disinfection. There have been no changes in sericulture yet. "Jinjiaqiao": Farmers in various villages have abandoned local silkworm eggs and are not raising them. There have been no changes in sericulture yet. Only because of the cold weather, the development of silkworms is delayed, and the early batches are only in the second molt and have plenty of leaves. "Wuxi": Less than one-third of the families in the four townships are raising silkworms. This is because of the repeated failures in sericulture over the years, which have suffered losses. Therefore, very few people are buying silkworm eggs. Various silkworm egg farms are reducing prices to seek sales. High-quality improved varieties such as Shouxing brand are only selling for one yuan per sheet. Lao Ci brand is nine cents, and Sanyuan Jinqian and other brands are only eight to seven cents. The livelihood of various silkworm egg sales shops remains bleak.

(Yokohama Raw Silk Plunges Repeatedly) Japan is now starting to raise spring silkworms, and new cocoons will soon be on the market. However, the stock of old silk is still large, so they are actively lowering prices to seek sales. The market price of Yokohama raw silk has plunged repeatedly. Ordinary Eight Arrow brand 13/15 denier is only opening at 540 yen, which is less than 480 yuan when converted to Chinese currency. Haibei brand 20/22 denier is only 505 yen, which is only 438 yuan when converted to Chinese currency. European and American silk merchants are still not making large purchases.

Qimen Black Tea Has New Production 287

Qimen black tea has always been known for its excellent quality. However, because it was picked too late, there was less fine tea and more coarse tea, which often led to unfavorable business. This year, the tea houses in Qi floating and other areas, in view of this, urged each tea household to pick tea earlier in advance. According to the letter report from Qizhuang, Shanli Likou and other places have already started picking and producing this week. Because the weather is clear, the tea buds are extremely fine and tender, and the fragrance is particularly excellent. Tea houses and manor houses are collecting green tea at 1.5 yuan per catty. In the future, the price for dried mature tea will be about 280 yuan per dan.

Women's Garden, Issue 10

The Evolution of Gender Relations 288

— Zi

Biologists tell us that life on Earth initially had no gender. It reproduced through cell division. Later, cells gradually had differences in size and activity, and there was what is called the difference between male and female. The combination of these two types of cells is called sexual reproduction. Female cells—ova—are often two to three thousand times larger than male cells—sperm. This is also evident in lower-level organisms, where females—such as female fleas and queen bees—are often larger than males. Moreover, female cells have the right to choose or reject male cells. Therefore, for males to please females, it is necessary to transform their bodies. For example, the males of higher animals are often more beautiful and magnificent than the females. This is the general evolution of gender relations in the animal kingdom. As for humans, after breaking away from the realm of apes and becoming the spirit of all things, gender relations are naturally different from all animals. Here is a historical account of the evolution of human gender relations:

(1) Primitive Age—Mother-Centered Age. After humans broke away from the animal realm of free sex, sexual intercourse was restricted—incest was forbidden. Thus, parents and children were distinguished, and society was born. However, at that time, floods and fierce battles were a major threat to humans. Therefore, men had to spend their days conquering abroad or wandering in other countries, with uncertain whereabouts and impermanent lives. For the sake of reproducing the race, women cultivated nearby and raised children, living a relatively stable life. Because of polyandry, children only knew their mothers. Women dominated everything, and maternal power was higher than everything else.

(2) Feudal Age—Father-Centered Age. Human power triumphed over nature. Men abandoned nomadic life for farming, and life gradually became stable. Land gradually became private property. Women specialized in production, raising children, or only assisting in cultivation and other domestic handicrafts. From this, economic power was entirely in the hands of men. Maternal power declined from this point on. Children took their father's surname, and paternal power replaced maternal power. Men dominated everything. Women thus became subordinates of men, becoming privately owned by men in the same way as livestock and land. From this, a male-centered feudal society was formed, creating all kinds of dogmas that imprisoned women. From this point on, women not only had no rights but also lost the status of "human." (3) Capitalist Age—Women's Dual Slavery Age. Since the Industrial Revolution in Europe in the late 18th century, machines have replaced human power, disrupting domestic handicrafts. On the one hand, men who were tenant farmers and laborers could not support themselves, let alone take care of their families. Therefore, women also left their homes to work as laborers and servants, at the mercy of others, exploited. From this, ordinary poor women, under the subjugation of men, became slaves of factories or masters—dual slaves! Or they became prostitutes.

(4) Gender Equality Age. The wheel of time is moving forward, and society is changing day by day. When things reach an extreme, they must revert. Women, living in this inhuman environment, must rise up to seek improvement. At the same time, some men will provide sympathetic assistance. At that time, men and women will be members of production, and no one will be enslaved by anyone else. Everyone has the freedom to choose a profession, and everyone has the freedom to love. Everyone has their own profession, and everyone has their own freedom. There are no resentful women, nor are there kept men. This is not a utopia; some countries are already practicing it.

Ancient China did not seem to lightly regard women. The myth of Nuwa patching up the sky with stones is proof that women have great abilities. Also, the theory of mother-centeredness is valid. However, since Confucian thought dominated people's minds, the idea of male superiority and female inferiority was more harmful than in any other country. The "Book of Changes" states, "The way of heaven creates the male, the way of earth creates the female. Heaven is superior, earth is inferior." It has long regarded women as doormats for men. The "Book of Songs" says, "If a son is born, he is laid on a bed, he plays with a scepter. If a daughter is born, she is laid on the ground, she plays with a tile." Women have been despised since childhood. There are also the long chains and short fetters of the three obediences and four virtues, which heavily lock women up. Fortunately, heaven and earth cannot lack women, or else Chinese women would have been completely assimilated by these teachings and returned to heaven long ago. For thousands of years, Wu Zetian managed to hold on, but she only did it for herself and did not awaken all women. She ultimately failed and did not help later women. In the past 30 years, the surge of the women's movement in Europe and the United States has also affected this ancient country in the Far East, and there has been a considerable response. However, most women are still living in a drunken stupor or like beasts of burden. The entire country of China is also under the heavy pressure of imperialism, and Chinese women are suffering from even heavier oppression. But I believe that when things reach an extreme, they must revert. People under heavy pressure, rise up! We do not hope that women will overwhelm all men and rebuild a mother-centered society. What we hope for is a truly equal society for men and women.

Talking About Tiles 289

— Bi Yao

The Book of Songs says: If a boy is born, give him a scepter (zhang) to play with; if a girl is born, give her a tile to play with. During the Song Dynasty, brothels were called tile houses (washe) or tile places (wazi). It seems that the character tile (wa) is often used for women. Sometimes, congratulating someone on the birth of a daughter is called "joy of playing with a tile," which completely represents women with tiles.

The difference between a seven-foot-tall man and a woman is like the difference between jade and tile. In ancient times, many heroes, in times of crisis and survival, often said a hard word: "Better to be jade shattered than a tile preserved." If you extend this from the perspective of playing with a scepter and playing with a tile, it means: Better to be a dead husband than a living woman.

In recent years, the country's situation has been precarious, collapsing and splitting apart, which is the time for men to shatter like jade. However, silently, few are heard of. Is it that there are very few husbands in society, and most of those alive are women?

This may be the real situation. No matter how much the country lacks statistics, it is known that there should be more women than men. Look, in addition to the flourishing of polygamy, brothels everywhere are increasing day by day. Moreover, the so-called wars against immortals and against foreigners, I am afraid that the work of cleaning up bandits requires the lives of men in most cases. If China were to organize a "husband-seeking corps" like Japan, it would be a magnificent sight. As for young widows, their husbands have already entered the earth, so they are not qualified to join this ranks. However, all these women who have lost their partners have not been deeply influenced by propriety, justice, and shame. They neither maintain chastity nor seek their late husbands. They flock to the "Peach Blossom River" and the "Beauty's Nest." The revolution has not yet succeeded, and women are not making any effort. This is a great sigh!

For these shameless women, those in high positions generally forgive them for being ignorant women; and those in humble positions mostly pity them for being at the end of their ropes. However, there are also some people who believe that this is women's revenge against men and the beginning of the women's movement. They think that men are the enemies of women, and any cruel means should be used against enemies. The best would be knives, saws, cauldrons, and tripods to deal with them. Unfortunately, these things are not available, so they have to use deception, manipulation, abandonment, betrayal, and other methods. Even if there is no problem with life, they should transform themselves into the Beauty's Nest. How wrong this view is, needs no discussion. Is the goal of these people to drive all men into the abyss and establish a so-called "country of women"? Fortunately, those who hold this view are only a very small number of ignorant women, and the Chinese nation will not be affected by it and be in danger.

However, what is frightening is that errors close to this kind are actually spreading in everyday social phenomena. Generally, it is to see the enemy who conflicts with oneself as heavy as Mount Tai and to see the entire big problem as light as a feather. Gather all one's heart and energy, and work every day to thoroughly treat what one calls an enemy. Deception and cruelty, no matter what method; men's lives are short, and their vitality is lost.

To exhaust this number is to see the number of "tile houses" increasing day by day, the signs of "disintegration" becoming clearer day by day, the wind of "tile houses" becoming more intense day by day, and the flow of "tile preservation" becoming more numerous day by day; it will be seen that everything is made of tile, and the whole country will become a pile of "rubble." This can be considered the victory of tiles!

Several First Aid Methods 290

— Youbai

People in the world are in danger of life at all times, so it is necessary for everyone to know important and convenient first aid methods. Now briefly describe as left: (1) Trauma, those who are injured or drowned by violent injuries often show a state of collapse, that is, weak pulse, pale face, heart failure, difficulty breathing, etc. At this time, the injured should be immediately laid flat on their back, making their whole body comfortable, and the head slightly lower. If they are still conscious, they can drink a small amount of ammonia wine. If they have lost consciousness, use cotton wool dipped in a small amount of ammonia and place it in front of their nose. The injured can restore consciousness by smelling it. The most important thing to pay attention to is that when consciousness disappears, it is most taboo to get cold. The injured must sleep in a warm place and put a hot water bag next to their side or feet, but it should not be too hot to avoid burns.

(2) If the wound is bleeding, use clean gauze or cloth strips to press down on the wound. If it still does not stop, use a rubber tourniquet with elasticity to tie it up. However, this method can only be used by those with experience. Otherwise, improper use can be harmful.

(3) If the skin is broken, do not touch it with your hands. Immediately use disinfected cotton wool dipped in iodine and other bactericidal drugs to apply to the wound, and then wrap it with clean gauze strips. If the injury is more serious, send it to the hospital.

(4) The most common first aid method for nosebleeds is to raise your head or sit up, breathe through your mouth, and cover the upper part of your nose with a cold water towel or ice pack. If it still does not stop, you should ask a doctor for help.

In short, first aid methods are all emergency temporary response methods. All serious injuries and illnesses are often transformed from small ones. There are many, many cases where dangerous symptoms are caused by unclean fingers or bandages, so it is best to go to the doctor for treatment as soon as possible.

A Woman's Heart 291

— First

People always say this: "You are too good." But, I want to receive judgments of "right" and "wrong." However, there is no absolute "right" and "wrong" judgment in the world; who is willing to tell me: "You are right" or "You are wrong?" Why "too good"? I understand: this is just a sigh of sympathy from the weak, if this one is my friend; otherwise, it is mocking me as a foolish idiot.

When my father knew of my unfortunate experiences, he said to me as if he were angry: "What did you do; you are really useless. You can't even hold onto your own husband!" Alas. Even my father doesn't understand my "heart"!

Not long after we fell in love, I learned that he had been passionately in love with another woman not long before we fell in love; but I don't know how he and she broke up. -- It is said that it broke up because she refused to agree to his demands.

After I told my best friend about all the things between him and me, she became worried for me: she thought that a man who had just come out of a passionate relationship would immediately be passionately in love with a second woman and forget the first woman so quickly, this man's feelings are too changeable, too easily transferred. She warned me: "Can you believe that he won't fall passionately in love with a third woman?" So I began to doubt, hesitate, I wanted to leave him. But he was so stubborn: he wrote an "insulting" article scolding my friends as despicable, scolding them for not destroying our love. Naturally, my friends left me in anger.

He earnestly dissected himself to me -- using various methods to express the sincerity of his heart. Finally, he concluded; he smashed the precious pipa that his teacher had given him; and told me: -- he also raised his hand to show me, a half-inch-long scar at the pulse on his wrist, covered with adhesive plaster -- he wanted to commit suicide, he had written a "blood letter" to me.

I looked at the broken pipa and the scar on his hand, I was very moved, very sad; I abandoned doubt, stopped hesitating, and became a prisoner of emotion, he wouldn't (or couldn't bear to let me)

see the "blood letter" he "said" he wrote, and I deeply believed that he had indeed done this tragic and foolish thing, and I was grateful for his sincere love for me; I never thought that he was using "death" to threaten an emotionally weak woman.

He finally gained victory: he "occupied" the second woman. We lived together for five years and had three children. Under the pressure of borrowing money, pawning things, and even living in hunger, we lived a life of conflicts of "sexual" disharmony and "temperament" disharmony: we often quarreled, and sometimes he even beat me; but we also often said, thinking; that we loved each other.

After five years, our life slowly improved economically; but our love, unknowingly, showed obvious cracks, although he still said that he loved me, and I believed that I loved him -- he had also told me that he loved my friend, my friend strictly rejected him, and later she got married, and this matter subsided for a long time. Not long before we separated, he had mentioned to me: he loved ××; but he immediately confessed to me and said: he shouldn't love other people. I also saw the strangeness in his treatment of me and the cracks between us, but I thought I shouldn't easily doubt him; I should trust him and understand him. Besides, he is a faithful man, who made an oath with "broken pipa", "suicidal wrist", and "written blood letter", would his "conscience" allow him to break his oath? -- However, I also thought: if our combination was a mistake from the beginning, and now he has discovered the disharmony between us, and at the same time he has found love elsewhere, he is willing to propose a divorce, I will definitely accept it; because I myself have long felt uneasy after living with him - not a simple problem of material lack -- but I still hope that we can all be patient, maybe for the sake of the children we will slowly live in peace.

I never expected that he would use deception to leave me and frame me, was he afraid that I would also use "death" to blackmail him? In the second month after I gave birth to my third child, he said to me: he had already planned it, he decided to go to Japan. I had heard him say many times: he said he had not read enough books, which was a lifelong regret. He wanted to find a way to go to Japan. Therefore, I believed and was very happy that he could fulfill his wish. In order to encourage his ambition, not wanting to burden him with family, I took three children, and according to his wishes, returned to my hometown -- Hunan. I thought: my task for him should be to help him in this way. Why didn't I doubt him? Guard against him? Because I thought "love" should "trust". Even if he set up a plan to leave me, what is the point of me not leaving him? If he sincerely loved me, this is a perfect touchstone. However, I still deeply believed: he will return from Japan in two years, as he said! He has a higher "position" in society, more "money"; we will have a very good life coming.

But not long after we left, he and another woman lived together in Shanghai; but I didn't know. He wrote to me still saying that he missed us very much; after a year and a half, I heard about their cohabitation from his new lover's family. When I wrote to him asking why he didn't openly tell me and discuss the issue of the three children, his reply was a frank admission; but he still said it in a repentant and extremely moving tone -- he said that he and she had a long history, and they had children, and he had fallen into a love net and could not escape. He said he still loved me and wanted to remarry me. He said he loved children too much, he liked having many children, and he still wanted to have children with me.

I got the story of him and her falling in love from her family, knowing that he again used the same old trick to occupy the third woman. -- Her father said to me? He said to her: if she didn't agree to his demands, he would "die". Therefore, she was finally occupied by him. He won again.

I have been separated from him for five years. In five years, our distance is as far as the north and south poles - he went to Fujian, I lived in Hunan for two years and then struggled to go to Beiping to make a living. In five years, I suffered all kinds of cruel abuse from society, struggling to support three children, he didn't help me. He wanted me to send the children to his hometown -- Zhejiang, to be taken care of by his seventy-year-old and sixty-year-old and sick parents. I couldn't bear to let three such young children suffer with two old people, I didn't do that. Last year, he returned from Fujian to Shanghai, and I went from Beiping to Nanjing, he wanted me to give him the children. I only gave him one. This year, he went to Shaanxi again, I heard from her that she was unwilling to bring my children. And the fact proved to me, his letter also proved: he doesn't need many children anymore - he and she have two more children - he doesn't love the children I gave birth to anymore.

He is a poor scholar wandering everywhere, and I am a weak and weaker woman, how will I deal with him?

For the sake of the three poor, unfortunate young ones, I think I should sacrifice everything of myself to take on this responsibility; although my own ability is so weak, and the future is so bleak! I cannot care about my own suffering, I do not hope for his help; I only ask for true sympathy in the world, and the final judgment of justice.

Why couldn't I initially reject his blackmail? After living together and feeling the conflicts in life, why couldn't I leave him? Why did I resolutely take the children home, deeply believing in him without doubting him? Why didn't I give the children to his parents? Why can't I abandon the children, and still take on such a difficult and arduous responsibility for him?

"You are 'too' good"! This is the only judgment I got from the world. People say: "The heart of a vicious woman", I hate why my heart is not "vicious"? Why not "poisonous"? I am actually a "weakling"!

Is there anyone willing to tell me: "You are right" or "You are wrong"?

After Marriage 292

— Lian Sheng

Marriage -- what a thought-provoking term!

Some people say "marriage is the graveyard of love", really, marriage is too painful and too boring for me. How much I curse the life of marriage! It can bury people's youth, it makes people lose their diligence, it gives people infinite sadness, negativity. At least, that's for me.

From friendship to love, from love to marriage with him, it took a full four and a half years, we understood each other's tendencies, understood each other's temperaments, knew that a combination was possible, and then we got married.

On the day of the ceremony, many friends praised our happy marriage. Many classmates showed envious eyes. Indeed, we matched so well, whether in academics, skills, or qualifications.

Let's look at the life after marriage, we loved each other so deeply that we couldn't bear to be apart. Unfortunately, he lost his job and sighed at home every day. I tried my best to comfort him, to make him happy, to ease his mind. At the same time, I dismissed the nanny and replaced her with my own operations.

As for him, he lost his mother at the age of thirteen, in order to make him relive the sweet love of a loving mother, I also represented his mother's love for him, he often said: since marriage, he has almost forgotten his mother, and no longer feels the pain of losing his mother. Sometimes, he seemed very annoyed and scolded me, I deeply understood his irritable temper and just didn't talk back, although, bitter tears flowed back into my stomach. (To be continued)

Opinions of Great World Thinkers on Women's Issues (3) 295

— Hua

Three. Wollstonecraft

Wollstonecraft (Mary Wollstonecraft) is also one of the great figures among the advanced warriors in the struggle for women's rights. She was British, born in 1759, the same era as Condorcet (see last issue of this journal). Condorcet was a genius propagandist and organizer of the women's movement in the era of the French Revolution; while Wollstonecraft was a writer who fought for women's rights with her pen. In her famous book "A Vindication of the Rights of Woman", her sharp writing style and passionate wording gave great excitement to the British women who had already awakened to freedom at that time.

Wollstonecraft was extremely poor in her childhood, and she helped her mother with housework, abandoning the happiness of childhood. But because of this, she developed a kind of ability, that is, in her youth, she tried her best to seek independent employment. She gradually moved from being a teacher in a small school, a trainer, a principal, to entering the field of writing - mainly pedagogy.

At that time, there was a political figure in England named Burke, who published a pamphlet slandering the French Revolution, and Wollstonecraft wrote "A Vindication of the Rights of Men" to refute it. It can be said that she fervently believed in the creed of the French Revolution.

Wollstonecraft was not only sensitive to political oppression, but also sensitive to the plight of the poor. In "A Vindication of the Rights of Men" and other works, she angrily attacked the king, calling him "a soulless puppet standing high in the court:" She attacked the declining aristocracy, attacked parasitic companions, and condemned the slave spirit of the standing army. She believes that the root of social evil lies in the division of society into classes. She said, "Poverty is the mother of crime and prostitution." "A Vindication of the Rights of Men" made Wollstonecraft's fame greatly increased, which aroused the reactionary forces' hatred for her. The brave Wollstonecraft was very firm; she tirelessly solidified the concept of social and political equality that she had realized in her heart. As a result of her hard work in research and thinking, she published "A Vindication of the Rights of Woman" in 1792. Her insights are higher and deeper than Condorcet's. She believes that allowing women to enjoy completely equal rights is not only the realization of an abstract concept of justice, but also a prerequisite for the highest development of personality and the full prosperity of women. She said that only political and economic liberation can enable women to freely and thoroughly solve the unique tasks of themselves.

Wollstonecraft said that women should not only receive equal education, unite with the highest aspirations of men, but also gain economic independence and get rid of dependence on men. Women's prostitution or marriage due to the oppression of poverty are not allowed.

She said that women who have lost their political rights and do not pay attention to the interests of the entire society will inevitably not be independent, and will become victims of superstition, and will definitely not wisely educate their children. The intelligence of women should be more than what it is now, otherwise, women cannot become virtuous mothers. "Women should be transformed from slaves in politics and civil rights into wise and free citizens. Try to let women enjoy all the happiness of education and manage the country like men, and then you will clearly see how smart and excellent women will be with their own liberation."

Wollstonecraft called the selfish love of motherhood, which is closed in a narrow family and isolated from the world, "animalistic love." She said that to train citizens, we must first have good female citizens. To make people's rights full, women need to elect their own representatives to participate in political institutions - the parliament, and not to ask about politics, "obey others' arbitrary decisions." But if the entire administrative system of the country is suitable for an autocratic regime, then women should not lament.

The main idea of "A Vindication of the Rights of Woman" is as described above.

In the conclusion of this book, she also established a great task for the women's world, that is to develop their buried talents and recognize their own strength. However, she said, if there is no equality in society, no elimination of the differences in the valve, and no liberation of women, then women will not be able to become excellent.

Shen Bao Amateur Weekly

Amateur Ramblings

An Exploration of the Shanghai Municipal Election System 296

— Gong Pu

Regarding the Shanghai municipal elections, reporters have repeatedly written articles for discussion, and the thirteenth representative congress of the Chinese Ratepayers' Association was held on the 16th. The Chinese members of the board of directors of the current Public Works Bureau have been elected. Although we have seen a rough picture of this election situation in the newspapers, there must be many people who do not understand the truth about whether this election system is appropriate. Therefore, I will give a brief description of the municipal election system and the Shanghai Municipal Election Regulations for discussion with the citizens of Shanghai.

Democratic politics is a better system in politics, which has been generally recognized by political scientists. The representative system is a way to realize democratic politics, and the representative system depends on the election system to express it, so all countries that adopt a democratic system attach importance to the election method. In the beginning, all advanced countries had various restrictions on elections, such as property, age, education, taxation, gender, etc. Later, they gradually evolved, and to this day, except for slight restrictions on age and education, they have all implemented universal suffrage. The so-called universal suffrage system means that all citizens who are nationals, are over 21 years old, have lived for a few months (different in each country), and are literate, can participate in the election, without any restrictions on property, taxation, gender, etc. Therefore, the qualifications of voters can be said to have been reduced to the lowest level, because without this, it is not enough to fully express the spirit of democracy.

The election methods are divided into direct and indirect. Direct elections use citizens to directly elect the people they want to elect, while indirect elections are where voters elect representatives, and then the representatives represent the election. Direct elections are mostly suitable for municipal areas with smaller areas and fewer populations, while indirect elections are the opposite. In the election, there are also so-called nominated candidates, that is, each election first nominates a number of candidates for citizens to choose and vote. This method can be applied to both direct and indirect elections, but the methods are slightly different in each country. The advantage of this is that it makes it easier for voters to follow, so that they do not vote blindly without any standards.

Municipal elections are sometimes divided into districts, and sometimes not. Voting mostly uses anonymous secret ballots. If a nomination system is used, the ballots are issued by the government for voters to fill in and cast into the ballot box, or they can be sent by the post office. In short, modern elections can be said to have become increasingly universal, fair, and convenient. In the beginning, we Chinese had no right to vote in the Shanghai Special Zone (i.e., the Public Concession) election. The board of directors of the Public Works Bureau only had foreigners, because Westerners generally had a misconception that the concession belonged to the foreigners, and only foreigners had the right to interfere in municipal affairs. But according to legal principles, this view is wrong. It was not until the 17th year of the Republic of China that the initiative of having Chinese directors was created, increasing from three to five. This process has been discussed in this journal and does not need to be repeated. Now, I will only discuss the election method of Chinese directors.

Only a part of Shanghai Chinese have the right to elect directors. There are strict restrictions on both voters and candidates. The qualifications of voters must have one of the following three: (1) Those who hold real estate worth more than 500 taels: (2) Those who pay more than 10 taels of property tax per year; (3) Those who pay more than 500 taels of rent per year and pay taxes. (The above-mentioned real estate must be in the Public Concession) The qualifications of candidates are (1) those who pay more than 50 taels of property tax per year, (2) those who pay more than 1,200 taels of rent per year and pay taxes. In addition to these two restrictions, candidates must have lived in the concession for more than five years. As for the election steps, the indirect system is adopted. First, those with the right to vote organize the Chinese Taxpayers Association to elect representatives, and then the representatives of the Taxpayers Association elect the directors. From this point of view, the election qualifications in the Shanghai Special Zone are completely focused on taxation and assets. People with a little common sense of modern politics cannot but feel regretful about this election system. "... If universal suffrage is implemented, not only we, but also foreigners, will dream of it." (See the speech of Mr. Wang Xiaolai at the Taxpayers' Association on the 16th) This kind of psychology is indeed a fact. However, this issue cannot be discussed at the moment, because the election of directors by our taxpayers is still restricted by the foreigners, and cannot be the same as the Western taxpayers' equal election, let alone others? Therefore, the next step should be to actively awaken the masses, train the masses, and constantly strive for progress based on the current situation. What is more, according to the facts, to take a step back, since the election is based on taxation, then in theory, taxpayers should have equal rights, and there should be no discrimination due to different nationalities; Chinese and Western citizens should jointly elect representatives. Of course, in fact, ethnic boundaries are inevitable, and moreover, the municipal administration of the concession is in the hands of foreigners, and elections in different nationalities are difficult to handle, but the Chinese taxpayers in the concession should have the right to vote, and no Westerners with any prejudice can deny it now. In this way, even if the Chinese and foreigners are separated to elect representatives, and each elects their own representatives, the number of directors should also be allocated according to the total amount of taxes paid by the Chinese and Westerners. The total amount of taxes paid by the Chinese accounts for more than 55% of the total revenue of the Public Works Bureau, so the number of representatives should be at least more than half. But what is it now? There are nine Western directors of the Public Works Bureau, but only five Chinese directors! European and American countries are advanced countries that have implemented democratic politics, but the Shanghai municipal administration controlled by Westerners has such an unreasonable election system, and there is such unequal treatment in the number of elected representatives from China and foreign countries. The reporter is not only worried about the implementation of the democratic system, but also about the future of international cooperation, which is fraught with unpredictable crises and should not be ignored.

Life

Rural Elementary School Teacher's Chalk Life 297

— Li Qing

The autumn wind blows, and the weather is delightfully refreshing. In the light green river, the water flows slowly and pleasantly. At this moment, two classmates and I were on a boat heading towards ×× village. We had just graduated from middle school, and we were about to go to ×× village to teach. Having not yet experienced the darkness of the world, we held beautiful fantasies about this future profession. We were eager to transform the current education system, to integrate the school and the countryside. We harbored boundless enthusiasm in our hearts, like a burning stove.

Needless to say, the 'chalk life' is not a happy one. You have to wake up early every day to lead the students in morning exercises; you have to rack your brains every day, spending energy and effort to lecture for seven or eight hours; and at night, you have to correct a lot of messy exercise books. And when Kid A punches Kid B, and Kid B comes crying to tell you, you have to lose your temper and hit Kid A a few times: Kid A's mother will then come and ask you why you hit her son... In short, when you are an elementary school teacher, you will be busy from morning till night. However, my two classmates and I didn't care about these things; we endured it all. And so, we continued to work.

We started by integrating with the students. After class, we played with the students.

'Come on, let's capture Mr. ×!' The innocent and lively children surrounded me and carried me to their prison.

In this way, we had a very good relationship with the students. Of course, we were very strict in class. We treated the students with both 'kindness and authority,' guiding them with emotional education, turning the entire school into a paradise, to the point that the children even came to school on Sundays.

Next, we broke the local feudal remnants of traditional concepts of men and women, eliminating the gender boundaries between students. Eventually, teachers, students, boys, and girls were all playing basketball together.

We helped the senior and intermediate grades produce wall newspapers, and we also published a picture wall newspaper for the lower grades. Whenever we saw countless small heads crowding in front of the wall newspaper, with pure eyes and simple rural smiles on their faces, we were so moved that we didn't know what to do, and we were so happy that we couldn't even smile.

Being with these pure children is unparalleled happiness. I went with them to 'general cleaning,' worked together, planted vegetable gardens together, traveled together...

When the setting sun was as red as fire, we often carried hoes and went to the vegetable garden with the children. Passing through fields and quiet woods, the birds sang

The Relative Ideological World and the New Life Movement 298

— Tie Min

In the current ideological world, its changes are truly endless, but the most obvious are 'modernization' and 'restoration of antiquity.' Novel and eccentric things are staged there every day, but they always escape these two paths, these two paths that develop in opposition to each other. The reason why the Chinese ideological world has this phenomenon is because the productivity of Chinese society does not develop, causing panic for the survival of the nation. The relations of production are, on the one hand, the restoration of ancient handicraft feudalism, and on the other hand, Europeanized capitalism. These two relative paths of economic life reflect the current relative ideological world.

What is the meaning of 'modern'? Simply put, it is decadent hedonism. Dancing, sports, and movies are the main ways this is displayed. Everything in life takes it as a dazzling standard. Men and women in universities walk into dance halls embracing each other, nude dancing performances in movie theaters sell out, and clothing is decorated according to female celebrities as the standard. Openings must also invite female celebrities. Therefore, modern women also learn the 'lewdness' and 'heat' of female celebrities to attract men. On the men's side, they are enthusiastic about sports. A portrait of a modern man is one wearing shorts, with bare arms, and wearing many medals, a person full of vanity and sensuality. Thus, the marriage of male athletes and female celebrities is regarded as the most modern combination.

The trend of the times is such that people who call themselves gentlemen sing the lament of deteriorating customs and morals, and come up with many old methods to save it, such as advocating the reading of scriptures movement, and someone petitioning the authorities to restore the old etiquette, and other significant facts.

The image of the ideological world entering two extremes has truly made the general youth dizzy. Calls for not being able to get through, and cries of annoyance and pain, can be heard everywhere. News of young people committing suicide because they have no way out in their thinking is also heard from time to time. If this phenomenon is still allowed to take its course, it will ultimately not be a blessing for the party and the country.

Now, the 'New Life Movement' promoted by our hardworking and meritorious party, military, and political officials is to correct this relative ideological world, eliminate 'modernization' and 'restoration of antiquity,' to start afresh with the people and be a pioneer for the people. All my people, let us rise up and support the 'New Life Movement.'

songs, in harmony with our 'rustling' footsteps. Ah, how poetic and great nature is! I was intoxicated...

'Don't move!' said the little friend in front. So, tiptoeing and gently squatting on the ground; in front of the small, white, chubby hands, a butterfly was perched. 'Haha! I caught it, it's a swallowtail butterfly. Let's take it back to make a specimen!'

We arrived at the vegetable garden, looking at those green and lovely vegetables, ah! That is our achievement.

'Mr. ×, we need to apply some fertilizer. We can eat it in another week.'...

This kind of life, one could live a lifetime without getting tired of it! We also got along with the farmers. In our busy lives, we founded a people's night school, setting aside two hours every night to teach at the night school and helping illiterate people learn to read. We opened the library and allowed people in the village to read newspapers and books. When we had important news, we published a 'people's wall newspaper' and posted it on the walls in the village.

In the evening, when the farmers had free time, they gathered under the trees to chat. 'Go, go and call the teachers to tell us stories!' In this way, the open-air lecture began again.

We also set up a 'People's Scribe Office' and a 'People's Inquiry Office' to serve the people in the village.

'Young, really good people!' What we received was the villagers' sincere gratitude. Although it was hard work, this kind of spiritual comfort was sweet.

Good times don't last forever. The local tyrants and evil gentry in the village gradually became dissatisfied with us, because we taught the farmers a lot of new knowledge, which they didn't like. After we encouraged the students to destroy the side room of the Guan Di Temple next to the school to make a library, they openly opposed us even more. These evil gentry created obstacles for us in everything. They spread many unpleasant rumors about us.

Did we want to add school supplies? The financial manager replied:

'Okay, later. It's not convenient with money now.'

The student football team went on an expedition and asked the school board for subsidies, but received an unreasonable rebuff.

In short, they messed up everything for us, and they made it impossible for us to develop anything. Finally, at the end of this semester, we had to end our teaching life.

'Mr. ×, don't leave! If you leave, we will have to live a dry and boring life again, we will no longer study!' Although the children tried to keep us in this way, the day we had to leave finally arrived.

'Mr. ×, don't forget us! Write us some letters!' When we got on the boat, the friends who saw us off on the dock said. From their bright eyes, on their red cheeks, dropped sparkling tears...

The wind was still blowing the same way, and the water was still flowing the same way, but it was winter weather. A thin layer of ice seemed to cover our warm hearts. Our beautiful fantasies turned into bubbles.

Sedan Chair Porters of Sichuan 299

— Ji Yu

'Creak, creak, creak, creak, two shoulders used as a horse'

This is a Sichuan fairytale, but it is what sedan chair porters least like to hear. I remember when I was young, I once took a sedan chair to my grandmother's house. On the way, the sedan chair bumped somehow and frightened me. I seemed to blame the sedan chair porters and casually hummed these two sentences. The sedan chair porters were very angry when they heard this and cursed: 'This short-lived ghost is hateful!'

Last year, when I returned to my hometown and took a sedan chair again, I encountered a sedan chair porter who deliberately gave me trouble. However, I couldn't bear to hum this 'shoulders used as a horse' tune anymore, even though their lives were actually worse than mules and horses!

Sedan chair porters in Sichuan are politely called 'carrying masters,' and bitterly scolded as 'killing mules' in a more vicious way. Because their scope of exertion is different, sedan chair porters are divided into three types: 'long shift,' 'extra shift,' and 'crossing street shift.'

'Long shift' specializes in soliciting long-distance business. They make their own sedan chairs. For example, from our × county to Chengdu, this 360-mile long journey requires hiring them. After the price is agreed upon, the sedan chair porters must be given 'tooth-beating festival' – eating wine and meat – the day before the passenger departs. Once on the road, the sedan chair porters are responsible for their own food and lodging, and the passenger does not care. On the road, they have to walk eight or ninety miles of rugged mountain roads every day. The wage is on average two hundred wen per mile – split equally by the two porters. They dare not eat their fill – it is said that eating their fill makes it difficult to carry the sedan chair. They can only eat a bowl of 'hat top' – a bowl of rice – with pickled vegetables four or five times a day. Each bowl of 'hat top' costs about four hundred wen. After each meal, they have to smoke one or two pans of opium, each pan costing five hundred wen. 'Check in before nightfall, and look at the sky early at cockcrow.' They can strictly abide by these two mottoes on the lanterns at the door of the inn without fail. Whenever the sky is about to darken, they rush to the station as if someone is whipping them from behind, to prepare a room for the guests, pack the luggage from the sedan chair into the room, and check the number. Then, they go to eat or smoke opium, waiting for the guests at the inn to arrive. They then pinch out two hundred wen to ask the 'young master' – the waiter at the inn – to bring them a bed of ragged and dirty bedding, which they each take to spread on the ground outside the threshold of the passenger's room, or at the base of the inn's counter, lying down like dry firewood to recover from their fatigue all day long. The next day, as soon as the east turns white, they immediately crawl out of their bedding, pack the sedan chair, and prepare to return to their journey where they cannot even eat their fill.

'Extra shift' is the generally known 'extra shift craftsmen.' They do not have their own sedan chairs. Every day, as soon as it is light, they squat in small shops next to the road – there is a small shop every five or six miles in Shu, selling cigarettes, tea, 'hat tops,' etc. Long-distance sedan chair porters may get tired, fail to reach the station, or get sick midway – sedan chair porters are most prone to heatstroke, stomach pain, and other illnesses. They then have to find 'extra shift' to carry the sedan chair for ten or eight miles. 'Extra shift' can only get one hundred and fifty or sixty wen per mile, and the remaining forty or fifty wen still goes to 'long shift.' They always carry the sedan chair back and forth on a certain section of the road, doing 'round-trip' business. When business is good, they earn even more money than 'long shift.'

'Crossing street shift' specializes in carrying business in the city. Their sedan chairs are purchased from guilds. Once they get business, the price is always a little higher than 'long shift' and 'extra shift,' earning four or five hundred wen per mile. However, in recent years, the economic panic has penetrated everywhere. Every city in Sichuan is inevitably facing an increase in the number of unemployed, and sedan chair porters must抢
