Commentary

Clothing and Social Life 300

— Lan

Recently, we often hear on newspapers compatriots advocating domestic goods opposing wearing Western clothes and news of destroying Western clothes. The reasons they oppose, roughly, are no different from what Mr. Tianxu Wosheng said the other day: 'Foreigners come to China to preach, and they still wear our Chinese clothes. We don't go to foreign countries to be foreign slaves, so why should we change to wearing Western clothes?'

Although I am not a wearer of Western clothes, I think that those who oppose wearing Western clothes, whether in terms of theory or method, are inevitably滑稽. I believe that advocating domestic goods and wearing Western clothes are not opposed. The reasons for the decline of the silk weaving industry are, on the one hand, affected by the global depression; on the other hand, it is because (1) China's tariffs cannot be completely autonomous, that is, it cannot use tariff barriers to prevent the import of foreign clothing materials, especially artificial silk, (2) Chinese silk weaving products cannot be improved, and (3) the bankruptcy of China's rural economy has reduced or even destroyed rural purchasing power.

If our tariffs can be completely autonomous and can prevent the import of foreign clothing materials, even if the Chinese change to wearing Western clothes, they can only use domestic materials, and there will be no outflow of profits. Why is China's national industry not actively urging the government to fight against imperialism and implement protectionist trade policies, but instead happily pointing fingers at compatriots who should not wear Western clothes? Isn't that strange?

Scolding Western clothes wearers as slaves who betray their country, if this can be used as a reason to oppose wearing Western clothes, it can only be applied to a part of people, that is, it applies to people who wear Western clothes as noble and glorious. If you use this reason to oppose the popularity of Western clothes and all Western clothes wearers, it is wrong.

In general, those who advocate Chinese clothes and oppose Western clothes, their biggest mistake is that they do not understand the relationship between clothing styles and social life. They do not know that clothing styles take an adaptive attitude towards social culture and life, which cannot be easily controlled by human power.

For example, why do monks, whether Chinese or foreign, always wear very loose and long clothes, while farmers and craftsmen often wear short clothes? The reason is: monks are people who do not work and eat, and even if they sometimes work, it is only mental, not physical. Therefore, the loose and long clothes they wear not only do not hinder them, but also show a special spirit and majesty. As for farmers and craftsmen, they are all physical laborers, and if they wear the clothes of monks, they will not be able to work at all. Therefore, they cannot but wear short and tight clothes.

We are now in the era of 20th-century mechanical civilization. All production uses machines, all transportation and traffic use machines, and even our daily life, sitting and lying, every move is related to mechanical civilization. Therefore, our clothing must take an adaptive attitude towards this mechanical civilization. Those millions of factory laborers standing in front of machines and those millions of engineers, drivers, chauffeurs, and sailors who deal with machines every day should pay close attention to the adaptability of their clothing styles to their working environment. It goes without saying that even general professionals such as doctors, clerks, company salesmen, and even ordinary residents, in this industrial civilization society, cannot but pay attention to the convenience of their clothing and its adaptability to social life. If you wear a Chinese robe and take a plane, or wear a Chinese palace dress and sit in a car, even if you can be careful and cautious, and escape the danger of life, you will inevitably feel great hindrance and inconvenience. Western-style clothing is the clothing that adapts to the 20th-century mechanical civilization society. If we want to pay attention to the lightness and comfort of clothing, we cannot but advocate Western-style clothing, or at least, we should not oppose Western-style clothing.

People change the environment around them, and therefore change themselves to adapt to the environment. We change from an agricultural society to an industrial society, and we must change to wearing industrial society's clothes, just as we change from an agricultural society to an industrial society, we must change our political system. Chinese robes and large-sleeved clothes actually illustrate that for thousands of years, the Chinese scholar-official class has been non-laboring. These clothes should have the same fate as the Chinese queue, and the people do not need to bother to speak. And now, there are still people in this 20th-century mechanical civilization society who advocate Chinese clothes and oppose Western clothes, which makes people feel puzzled.

抢 business to succeed. Those who do not know how to搶 will not have customers all day long. A sedan chair porter in Chongqing complained: it is difficult to earn one yuan a day, but regardless of whether there is business or not, the sedan chair shop owner must collect five吊 'rental money' every day – ten吊 of copper coins are exchanged for one yuan in Sichuan.

The dozen or so吊 they earn every day is only enough to eat 'hat top' rice and smoke opium – there are no sedan chair porters in Sichuan who do not smoke opium. Wearing straw sandals and resting in inns is barely enough, but in recent years, they have invented the 'sedan chair bar tax' to be collected from the sedan chair porters! If it is said that sedan chair porters can also have the opportunity to donate a special tax and knock off a kind of extra 'fortune,' then it is in the hot summer, when a female passenger inadvertently leaves a little menstrual blood on the seat board, then they have to敲 you at least three or five吊, especially if she is dressed nicely.

Employee Self-cultivation

Harmony Generates Wealth 301

— Translated by Shen Yi Wu

When I was walking along Fifth Avenue in New York that afternoon, I remembered that I needed to buy a stiff collar. So I stepped into a general merchandise store and explained to the clerk that I wanted to buy a stiff collar. He took one out of the box and showed it to me.

'This is the last one,' he sighed. At the same time, he pointed to the stiff collar he was wearing. This was indeed undeniable, the stiff collar was the same as his.

I really liked this stiff collar, so I asked the price.

'One dollar each.' This was the young clerk's reply, and at the same time he yawned. In fact, because of my weak economic ability, I was reluctant to buy a stiff collar for one dollar each. So I said to the clerk, please change it to one that costs two and a half角. As soon as I finished saying this, the clerk showed an unhappy look.

'Ah...' he said, with a bitter smile on his face: 'We don't have this kind of stiff collar, we have never had this kind of goods.'

'You will never buy such cheap goods on this Fifth Avenue street.' After he added this sentence, he took in the box, as if this matter was over. After thinking carefully, this kind of clerk is really unreasonable. He thought that I would never buy this two and a half角 stiff collar, which is really nonsense. Because I was able to buy it later, which really made his store able to 'close its doors.'

I went to the second store to try, and the clerk told me that they did not have any stiff collars cheaper than seven and a half角. However, his attitude towards customers was completely kind and amiable, and he expressed his apologies to me.

'We often see that general customers are attracted by high prices,' he explained to me this way: 'They think that good goods are not cheap, and cheap goods are not good. This concept is fundamentally wrong. Countless white nobles are using this kind of cheap stiff collar.'

After hearing his words, you may think that this clerk does not know the threshold for doing business. In fact, it is not so. In my opinion, he is indeed a polite salesman, because he pleases people with his amiable appearance, which makes me have to spend money to buy one.

I firmly believe that a certain large branch store is on the verge of bankruptcy, even though it was quite reputable in the whole town in the year it was opened. And I have calculated that the only reason for his failure lies in 'losing the public.' The prices of various goods in his store were all reasonable and fair, but because customers wanted to exchange a chair clock after buying it home, the clerks showed a kind of embarrassing appearance. They often checked the goods and said: 'I don't know about this' to perfunctorily deal with customers.

So the customers said to themselves hatefully: 'I hope I will never step into this kind of shop for profit again.'

A large grocery store firmly remembers the creed of showing humility to customers. They often say to customers: 'Thank you, please come again next time.' No matter how bad the customers' temper is, or even if they insult the clerks for no reason, they have to silently admit their mistakes. For example, the clerk should use euphemistic words when refusing to use inferior coins or counterfeit foreign coins. If a customer pays you a lead coin, you must not scold him, you should say to him with a gentle attitude: 'There are a lot of lead coins on the market now, sir, I don't know where one got mixed in...'

There is no more surprising example of generating wealth through harmony than the hotel industry. The first person to realize this fact should be George Paner, of today's Rainbow. Until his death, he was still recognized as a major traveler in the hotel industry.

'Politeness is the cheapest thing in the world,' Paner often said: 'But it is not easy to buy, it requires a great price.'

Paner insisted on the rule that the customer is always right. This rule is now widely used. For example, if a guest at a banquet says that the fish tastes bad and tells the waiter that the fish is spoiled, the waiter, although he firmly believes that the fish is not spoiled, must not retort to the customer: 'Where is it spoiled?' He must quickly remove the fish basin and politely ask the customer: 'Sir, what dish shall I replace it with?'

Paner daily wrote down the list of sick travelers on the table. If it was a serious illness, he would immediately go to his room to comfort his illness. If it was a woman, he would also send her a bunch of flowers.

There is also a small grocery store with this kind of harmony attitude. I once bought a postcard from it. I gave him a nickel coin and he gave me four cents change, and also said 'Thank you', as if this was a big business. I asked him the reason why he was so polite, and the manager explained to me: 'This is one of our store rules. We do not dislike retail buyers. Because using a pleasant attitude towards him will make him come again next time. Patronize.'

Many public service companies, such as gasoline and electric light companies, often treat dissatisfied customers with a kind of 'what are you doing here' attitude. However, today it has completely changed. They have hired inspectors in their stores, specializing in teaching these employees who do not treat customers well.

Everyone can recall the impolite wording of large companies' billing statements a few years ago, which have all been changed today. Like this kind of majority:

'...Your esteemed account may have been forgotten due to your busy affairs. We hereby re-mention it, hoping that you will pay it as soon as possible.'

Movie theaters should also be like this. When a woman comes late and there are no seats in the hall, the ticket seller must not say the lost sentence, 'The downstairs is full!' You should say to her very harmoniously: 'Madam, there are seats upstairs, priced at two yuan and two and a half yuan. ' Because people always like to hear pleasant words, and are not used to hearing hard-nosed words.

Scientific Talk

The Story of an Airplane 302

— Ge Ming

Before Christmas, my wife asked the children what clothes they wanted for the New Year, planning to have them made. My six-year-old daughter, Huzi, answered without hesitation, "I want a flight attendant uniform, I want to be a female aviator." We all laughed at the time, but we actually listened to her and had a leather suit made for her, and even bought her a small airplane.

Why did this child develop the idea of becoming an aviator? It's not without reason. First, of course, is curiosity. Aviators can go to the sky, and those who can go to the sky are naturally extraordinary people. She also often heard people say that there are female aviators in foreign countries, so she also wants to be someone above others. Second, naturally, it was the terrifying impact of the January 28th Incident. Although she was only four years old at the time and didn't understand the horrors of war, she had heard many war stories. She knew that Japan had more airplanes than China, and the Chinese air force didn't really fight Japan that time, which made her feel very indignant, and she felt she had to become an aviator. Third, it should also be attributed to the aviation atmosphere in the country in recent years. We often hear about foreign airplanes coming to China to perform, and we hear the miscellaneous sounds of airplanes in the sky every day, which naturally deepened her interest.

The parents of the aspiring aviator had to find popular materials, learning themselves while giving the children more accurate concepts. As a result, our family often had aviation conversations, and we had a small, armed female aviator and a small airplane.

My fourth younger brother studies airplane manufacturing, and he cleverly says that he can also fly them himself. Unfortunately, he is far away in Lingnan and can't come to our house often. However, in the children's minds, their fourth uncle is naturally stronger than their father. He is someone to be admired. In order to satisfy the children's wishes, when my fourth brother recently returned to our hometown, the first time I saw him, I told him about the children's admiration and invited him to give an aviation lecture to the children at our house. The following is his conversation with the children.

"Fourth Uncle! How can airplanes fly? Who came up with the idea?"

"Airplanes aren't really that strange. Birds soar through the clouds and fly high in the sky. Didn't they learn aviation tens of millions of years ago? If birds can learn it, humans certainly can too! The current airplanes were thought of from the fact that birds can 'fly'. They all use a special method to manipulate the air and ensure flight. You must know that all inventors in the world are not just daydreaming. They carefully observe everything and invent things for practical use. For example, scale insects, bees, flies, bats, and birds are all teachers of mankind. They were the earliest aviators, and humans learned the art of 'artificial flight' from their flying. It's very common."

"Birds' bodies are light! How can airplanes, such heavy things, fly? I really don't understand?"

"Haha! Do you think light things can fly? Ants are lighter than birds' bodies, and centipedes are lighter than scale insects. Why can't they fly? On the contrary, weight is a necessary condition for flight. Anything that can fly must be heavier than air. If birds were lighter than air and flew, then a strong wind would blow them away to who knows where. How could they fly back and forth freely? Do you understand?"

"I still don't understand. There are many things heavier than air! Why can't they fly?"

"I said that weight is only one condition. Besides weight, you also need appropriate flight organs and strength. Birds have weight, appropriately constructed flight organs, and can generate appropriate force to interact with the air, so they can fly. Airplanes are the same. If there isn't a proper combination, they can't fly. Birds' surfaces are naturally reduced to a minimum, but they can increase their active surface by vibrating their wings when necessary. When the wings vibrate rapidly, they turn the space they pass through into a strong foundation to support their bodies. The speed of the wing vibration must be higher than the speed of any wind. This way, it can control the wind and fly in any direction in the wind. Don't we often see birds' wings constantly vibrating in strong winds? Eagles, who are in the clear blue sky, just spread their wings and are too lazy to vibrate. That's the reason. However, birds' flight organs are active wings. Humans have now changed to propellers. Its purpose is the same: to attack and subdue the air, not to be attacked and subdued by the air."

"Fourth Uncle, why can airplanes fly upside down and fly tilted?"

"This is the same as how ships need to tilt when sailing. It's about controlling the air. The vibration of the wings in the air is like the oars of a boat in the water. 'When the wings flap downward, they strike downward and forward, and when they flap upward, they strike upward and forward, drawing a figure '8' in the air.' Airplanes also adopt this principle."

The child was listening with great interest, but was interrupted by dinner. This lecture made the child feel closer to birds.

Special Article

Eugenics and the Nation 303

— Chen Tianhua

Since Hitler came to power in Germany, he has been strengthening the military, working hard to govern, and trying to restore the national destiny shackled by the Treaty of Versailles. Recently, he has also formulated eugenics laws in order to improve the race and benefit future world wars. According to a Havas news dispatch on the 15th:

"Germany previously promulgated eugenics laws, prohibiting people with weak bodies, criminal records, or mental illnesses from marrying, so that bad seeds would be cut off from now on; and healthy races would become stronger. After the order was issued, the whole country followed. Now, in order to make the implementation of this order more closely supervised, all doctors and judges in the country will be given special education... The Saxon state government firmly believes that the Nordic people are uniquely blessed by nature. In terms of the spiritual and physical value given by the Creator, the components of the Nordic people are 'superior components'. Therefore, it plans to establish a research institute specializing in racial studies and national health in Dresden..."

Eugenics and national hygiene are originally related. The seeds of plants and animals can be artificially improved, so there is no reason why the human race cannot be improved. The concept of "selection" is not only applicable to the natural world, but also to humans. And heredity is the most important key to selection. Since Mendel's law of heredity came out, we know that heredity has quantitative laws to follow; since Weismann's theory of germ plasm came out, we know that heredity has a material basis to rely on. From this, eugenics becomes completely possible. Understanding this, it is very natural that the eugenics movement is promoted by nationalists. But there are debatable points in Germany's eugenics law. Physical weakness is not necessarily congenital. Malnutrition and disease are often the biggest causes of weakness. Furthermore, weakness is not absolutely unchangeable. If it were unchangeable, what would be the use of various sports, competitions, and boxing? Criminals are not necessarily unhealthy people, and there are extremely intelligent people among criminals. Moreover, the reasons for their crimes are mostly due to social evils and economic oppression. As for people with mental illnesses, although most of their nerves are unhealthy, the source of their illness is mostly acquired and not incurable. Moreover, there are extremely intelligent geniuses among the patients. If we cut off their reproductive functions for these people, it would be cruel in terms of humanity, oppression of the people in terms of politics, and a loss in terms of national interests.

But Hitler's vision is different. He believes that "dragons beget dragons, phoenixes beget phoenixes, and smart and healthy people beget smart and healthy people." He wants to use his eugenics law to make the German nation strong. He is completely taking the interests of the country as the premise.

I am not against eugenics, but I am not satisfied with this deformed eugenics. Instead of promoting this kind of eugenics, we should promote a superior environment. First, these eugenics activists often have wrong ideas, viewing the dominant figures in current society as humans who are fit for survival, believing that only the upper class should reproduce, while the majority of people are ignored. Eugenics is an aristocratic science from this point of view.

Second, these eugenics activists are manufacturers of war. Their advocacy of racial improvement is aimed at obtaining more strong soldiers and seizing other people's land and conquering colonies with greater certainty. Hitler's strict implementation of eugenics laws and Mussolini's encouragement of marriage can all be explained in this sense.

Third, instead of striving for racial transformation, we should strive for economic transformation. We cannot deny the right to life of human beings, and we see that economic transformation contributes more to mankind than other efforts. If we improve the environment for mankind, human society will naturally progress, and the human race will naturally tend towards evolution.

In our country, the remaining feudal consciousness shrouds society. The concept of social status, wealth, and poverty in marriage already contains the meaning of eugenic selection, as if it understands the meaning of eugenics. However, our nation is still decadent and lewd. Seeing that promoting eugenics will inevitably lead into a dead end, we should still strive to transform the nation's economic environment.

A Glimpse of the Recent World Economy

— Fanfu

Although it is said that the world economic panic is still deepening, when we review the various statistics of the world economy in 1933, the facts are somewhat different. If you don't believe me, please see:

Index of Industrial Production in 1933

1932 1933

United States 57.7 69.3

United Kingdom 88.4 91.7 (Average of July, August, and September) Germany 61.2 68.6 France 75.6 84.6 Japan 107.9 139.4 (November)

The index of industrial production is generally used by economists as a compass for economic conditions. If the production index is high, it means that industry is developed and the economy is prosperous, thus forming prosperity. Conversely, if the production index is lower than before, it means that production is depressed and the economy is exhausted, thus forming a recession. The above production index table is calculated using the production index of 1928 as the base. According to the table, the production indexes of the five major capitalist countries, the United States, Britain, Germany, France, and Japan, in 1933 were all higher than the indexes of the previous year. Therefore, some economists excitedly shouted, "The recession is about to pass, and prosperity is coming soon!"

Not only does the production index show the hope of improvement, but prices in various countries also show an upward trend. Look:

Index of Commodity Prices in 1933 (Wholesale)

1932 1933

United States 92 94*

United Kingdom 86 86 Germany 96 93 France 83 79 (December) Japan 121 135

Like the production index, commodity prices are also regarded as a compass for economic conditions. If commodity prices fall compared to before, it indicates overproduction and a reduction in social consumption, thus indicating a recession. If commodity prices rise compared to before, it indicates an increase in social demand, thus indicating signs of prosperity. The above commodity price index table uses 1913, the year before the war, as the base. This table tells us that commodity prices in major capitalist countries are almost all rising together. Therefore, optimistic economists shouted again, "The world economy has now moved from a recession to a sluggish stage!" After sluggishness comes prosperity.

But has the world recession really passed? Here we have to make a calm observation.

First, let's talk about the expansion of production. Although the average index for the whole year of 1933 was higher than that of 1932, this rise was unusually volatile. The production indexes of the major capitalist countries in the first half of 1933 almost all rose consistently, but once it reached June, the production indexes of the countries began to decline again. Japan was the earliest (June), followed by France (July), followed by the United States (August), and then Germany (September).

This fully proves that the expansion of production in 1933 was only a temporary expansion. This expansion was entirely stimulated by the artificial policies of various governments. When it reached a certain point, it would eventually reveal its true colors.

In fact, if we take off the signboard of "production expansion" and pay attention to the continued increase in the number of unemployed people and the continued reduction in workers' wages, then we can conclude that this expansion of production will never be sustained.

Now let's analyze the abnormal rise in commodity prices. The increase in commodity prices in various countries is also entirely due to the "commodity price recovery policy" of various governments. Under this policy, the first step is to increase tariffs or prohibit the import of foreign goods in order to form a monopoly price for domestic goods. In addition to this method, various monetary policies, such as stopping gold redemption and devaluing gold currencies, are used to raise nominal commodity prices. The high prices in the price index table for Britain, the United States, and Japan are due to this. Because Germany and France did not devalue their currencies, commodity prices showed a decline. Therefore, the increase in the commodity price index is ultimately just an illusion of various governments.

Not only has the world recession not passed, but it has become increasingly deepened due to this false expansion of production and the false rise in commodity prices. On the reverse side of production expansion are: overproduction, accumulation of military supplies, etc.; on the reverse side of the rise in commodity prices are: increasingly fierce international commodity wars and international currency wars. It is feared that the transition from economic war to armed war will eventually be unavoidable!

Biography of a Famous Person

Marconi, Inventor of the Wireless Telegraph (3) 305

— Senran

Marconi's research progressed day by day. In July 1897, he left the hands of Preece and established the Marconi Wireless Telegraph Company with a capital of one million yuan, and invited J.A. Fleming as a consultant. In 1898, he was again ordered to establish wireless telegraph receiving and sending stations between the Isle of Wight and Bournemouth, a distance of twelve miles. In August of the same year, the sick British Crown Prince (The Prince of Wales) and Queen Victoria often communicated by wireless telegraph, and Marconi was responsible for their communication, which attracted the greatest attention of the British people at that time.

The wireless telegraph communication between Queen Victoria and the Crown Prince was 30 miles long. Marconi's success here can be said to be a leap forward in the process of his invention of the wireless telegraph. In this wireless telegraph device, there was an Antenna pole standing on the coast that was 105 feet high, and an Antenna that was 83 feet long, which at that time had to be said to be a surprising creation.

At this time, people were holding a rowing competition. However, the final point of the competition was set in the ocean 20 miles away. People who went to watch the competition by boat could naturally immediately know the news of the victory or defeat, but the audience on the shore had to wait until the boat returned to know. At this time, the audience with fanatical emotions was naturally not very happy. Therefore, a news agency took the opportunity to use Marconi's wireless telegraph. As a result, the news of the final point 20 miles away could be immediately transmitted by wireless telegraph. As a result, the unhappy feeling of the fanatical audience was immediately eliminated. -- This was the first time that the wireless telegraph was used for ordinary application, and it was also the beginning of Marconi's fame in Britain.

In 1899, at the request of the French government, Marconi engaged in communication experiments across the English Channel between England and France. He erected a 150-foot-high Antenna in Dover, England and Wimereux, France, and used a wavelength of 12,000 meters. The result was a great success, and wireless telegraph communication across the English Channel was realized. As a result, there were increasingly practical opportunities for rapid communication between ships at sea and ships on the coast. At that time, there were already lightships equipped with wireless telegraph devices to rescue steamships that had run aground in dense fog. This was an example.

The most interesting and complete experiment of Marconi's maritime communication was during British naval exercises. Because the exercise required wireless telegraph communication, Marconi seized this opportunity and worked hard. In the autumn of one year, during a major exercise by the British Navy, he successfully established communication between the two ships Europa and Jarrow, which were 60 nautical miles apart. Later, the British Navy continued to pay him a royalty of 200,000 yuan for using the wireless telegraph he invented.

In 1899, the South African War broke out. Marconi's assistant also went to the battlefield, and Marconi's wireless telegraph actually rescued the isolated state of the South African besieged army in January 1900. This was the first time that the wireless telegraph showed its power in the military. (To be continued)
